USERMESSAGE #14
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     2→// Object State Machine Engine
     3→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     4→//
     5→// Objects are defined as JSON with state machines. Each state can have:
     6→//   - visual: string descriptor for renderer
     7→//   - particles: optional particle effect name
     8→//   - emoji: optional emoji to float on enter
     9→//   - auto_next: { state, after (seconds) } — timed auto-transition
    10→//   - transitions: { action_name: { next, duration?, requires?, produces?, target? } }
    11→//
    12→// The engine ticks all objects, advancing auto_next timers.
    13→// Characters trigger transitions via interact(objectId, action).
    14→
    15→export class ObjectInstance {
    16→  constructor(def) {
    17→    this.id = def.id;
    18→    this.name = def.name;
    19→    this.sector = def.sector;
    20→    this.arena = def.arena;
    21→    this.position = { ...def.position };
    22→    this.states = def.states;
    23→    this.state = def.state || Object.keys(def.states)[0];
    24→    this.timer = 0; // ms elapsed in current state
    25→    this.autoNextDuration = this._getAutoNextDuration(); // ms until auto-transition (null if none)
    26→  }
    27→
    28→  _getAutoNextDuration() {
    29→    const stateDef = this.states[this.state];
    30→    if (stateDef?.auto_next) {
    31→      return stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000; // convert seconds → ms
    32→    }
    33→    return null;
    34→  }
    35→
    36→  get currentStateDef() {
    37→    return this.states[this.state];
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  get visual() {
    41→    return this.currentStateDef?.visual || this.state;
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  get particles() {
    45→    return this.currentStateDef?.particles || null;
    46→  }
    47→
    48→  get timeRemainingMs() {
    49→    if (this.autoNextDuration === null) return null;
    50→    return Math.max(0, this.autoNextDuration - this.timer);
    51→  }
    52→
    53→  // Returns a transition event if auto_next fires, or null
    54→  tick(deltaMs) {
    55→    if (this.autoNextDuration === null) return null;
    56→
    57→    this.timer += deltaMs;
    58→
    59→    if (this.timer >= this.autoNextDuration) {
    60→      const autoNext = this.currentStateDef.auto_next;
    61→      return this._transition(autoNext.state, 'auto');
    62→    }
    63→
    64→    return null;
    65→  }
    66→
    67→  // Attempt a character-triggered interaction.
    68→  // Returns a transition event, or null if no valid transition.
    69→  interact(action = 'use') {
    70→    const stateDef = this.currentStateDef;
    71→    if (!stateDef?.transitions) return null;
    72→
    73→    const transition = stateDef.transitions[action];
    74→    if (!transition) return null;
    75→
    76→    // If the transition requires a character, that's expected (caller is a character)
    77→    return this._transition(transition.next, action, transition);
    78→  }
    79→
    80→  _transition(nextState, trigger, transitionDef = null) {
    81→    const prevState = this.state;
    82→    const prevVisual = this.visual;
    83→
    84→    this.state = nextState;
    85→    this.timer = 0;
    86→    this.autoNextDuration = this._getAutoNextDuration();
    87→
    88→    return {
    89→      objectId: this.id,
    90→      objectName: this.name,
    91→      from: prevState,
    92→      to: nextState,
    93→      trigger,
    94→      visual: this.visual,
    95→      particles: this.particles,
    96→      emoji: this.currentStateDef?.emoji || null,
    97→      produces: transitionDef?.produces || null,
    98→      target: transitionDef?.target || null,
    99→      timestamp: Date.now(),
   100→    };
   101→  }
   102→
   103→  // Force-set state (e.g., when another object's transition produces something here)
   104→  setState(newState) {
   105→    if (!this.states[newState]) return null;
   106→    return this._transition(newState, 'external');
   107→  }
   108→
   109→  toJSON() {
   110→    return {
   111→      id: this.id,
   112→      name: this.name,
   113→      state: this.state,
   114→      visual: this.visual,
   115→      particles: this.particles,
   116→      timer: this.timer,
   117→      timeRemainingMs: this.timeRemainingMs,
   118→      sector: this.sector,
   119→      arena: this.arena,
   120→      position: this.position,
   121→    };
   122→  }
   123→}
   124→
   125→export class ObjectEngine {
   126→  constructor() {
   127→    this.objects = new Map();    // id → ObjectInstance
   128→    this.listeners = [];         // event subscribers
   129→  }
   130→
   131→  addObject(def) {
   132→    const obj = new ObjectInstance(def);
   133→    this.objects.set(obj.id, obj);
   134→    return obj;
   135→  }
   136→
   137→  addObjects(defs) {
   138→    for (const def of defs) {
   139→      this.addObject(def);
   140→    }
   141→  }
   142→
   143→  get(objectId) {
   144→    return this.objects.get(objectId);
   145→  }
   146→
   147→  getAll() {
   148→    return [...this.objects.values()];
   149→  }
   150→
   151→  getBySector(sector) {
   152→    return this.getAll().filter(o => o.sector === sector);
   153→  }
   154→
   155→  // Advance all object timers by deltaMs.
   156→  // Returns array of transition events that fired.
   157→  tick(deltaMs) {
   158→    const events = [];
   159→
   160→    for (const obj of this.objects.values()) {
   161→      const event = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   162→      if (event) {
   163→        events.push(event);
   164→        this._handleProduction(event);
   165→      }
   166→    }
   167→
   168→    // Notify listeners
   169→    for (const event of events) {
   170→      this._emit(event);
   171→    }
   172→
   173→    return events;
   174→  }
   175→
   176→  // Character interacts with an object.
   177→  // Returns transition event or null.
   178→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   179→    const obj = this.objects.get(objectId);
   180→    if (!obj) return null;
   181→
   182→    const event = obj.interact(action);
   183→    if (event) {
   184→      this._handleProduction(event);
   185→      this._emit(event);
   186→    }
   187→
   188→    return event;
   189→  }
   190→
   191→  // Handle "produces" side-effects (e.g., oven done → bread in display_case)
   192→  _handleProduction(event) {
   193→    if (event.produces && event.target) {
   194→      const targetObj = this.objects.get(event.target);
   195→      if (targetObj) {
   196→        // Map production to a state on the target object
   197→        const targetEvent = targetObj.setState(event.produces);
   198→        if (targetEvent) {
   199→          targetEvent.trigger = `produced_by:${event.objectId}`;
   200→          this._emit(targetEvent);
   201→        }
   202→      }
   203→    }
   204→  }
   205→
   206→  onTransition(callback) {
   207→    this.listeners.push(callback);
   208→    return () => {
   209→      this.listeners = this.listeners.filter(l => l !== callback);
   210→    };
   211→  }
   212→
   213→  _emit(event) {
   214→    for (const listener of this.listeners) {
   215→      listener(event);
   216→    }
   217→  }
   218→
   219→  // Snapshot of all objects for debugging/display
   220→  snapshot() {
   221→    const result = {};
   222→    for (const [id, obj] of this.objects) {
   223→      result[id] = obj.toJSON();
   224→    }
   225→    return result;
   226→  }
   227→}

   136→// ── Sprite preloader ──
   137→function loadImage(src) {
   138→  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   139→    const img = new Image();
   140→    img.onload = () => resolve(img);
   141→    img.onerror = () => reject(new Error(`Failed to load: ${src}`));
   142→    img.src = src;
   143→  });
   144→}

   146→/**
   147→ * Preload all tile, object, and character sprites.
   148→ * Returns { tiles: Map, objects: Map, characters: Map }
   149→ * Failed loads are silently skipped (renderer falls back to colored rects).
   150→ */
   151→export async function preloadSprites() {
   152→  const tiles = new Map();
   153→  const objects = new Map();
   154→  const characters = new Map();
   155→  const props = new Map();
   156→
   157→  const promises = [];
   158→
   159→  // Tile sprites
   160→  for (const [tileId, path] of Object.entries(TILE_SPRITES)) {
   161→    promises.push(
   162→      loadImage(path)
   163→        .then(img => tiles.set(Number(tileId), img))
   164→        .catch(() => { /* fallback to color */ })
   165→    );
   166→  }
   167→
   168→  // Object sprites
   169→  for (const [visual, path] of Object.entries(OBJECT_SPRITE_PATHS)) {
   170→    promises.push(
   171→      loadImage(path)
   172→        .then(img => objects.set(visual, img))
   173→        .catch(() => { /* fallback to color */ })
   174→    );
   175→  }
   176→
   177→  // Character sprites
   178→  for (const [key, path] of Object.entries(CHARACTER_SPRITE_PATHS)) {
   179→    promises.push(
   180→      loadImage(path)
   181→        .then(img => characters.set(key, img))
   182→        .catch(() => { /* fallback to color */ })
   183→    );
   184→  }
   185→
   186→  // Prop sprites
   187→  for (const [key, path] of Object.entries(PROP_SPRITES)) {
   188→    promises.push(
   189→      loadImage(path)
   190→        .then(img => props.set(key, img))
   191→        .catch(() => { /* fallback — props just won't render */ })
   192→    );
   193→  }
   194→
   195→  await Promise.all(promises);
   196→  return { tiles, objects, characters, props };
   197→}
   198→
   199→export class Renderer {
   200→  constructor(container) {
   201→    this.canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
   202→    this.canvas.width = MAP_W;
   203→    this.canvas.height = MAP_H;
   204→    this.ctx = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
   205→    this.ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
   206→
   207→    // CSS scaling — fill window, keep aspect ratio
   208→    this.canvas.style.display = 'block';
   209→    this.canvas.style.imageRendering = 'pixelated';
   210→
   211→    // High-res text overlay canvas (renders at display resolution for crisp text)
   212→    this.textCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
   213→    this.textCanvas.style.position = 'absolute';
   214→    this.textCanvas.style.top = '0';
   215→    this.textCanvas.style.left = '0';
   216→    this.textCanvas.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
   217→    this.textCtx = this.textCanvas.getContext('2d');
   218→
   219→    this._resize();
   220→    window.addEventListener('resize', () => this._resize());
   221→
   222→    container.appendChild(this.canvas);
   223→    container.appendChild(this.textCanvas);
   224→
   225→    // Sprite caches (populated by setSprites)
   226→    this.tileSprites = null;      // Map<tileId, Image>
   227→    this.objectSprites = null;    // Map<visualKey, Image>
   228→    this.characterSprites = null; // Map<spriteKey, Image>
   229→
   230→    // Pre-rendered tilemap (offscreen canvas, re-drawn only when sprites load)
   231→    this._tilemapCache = null;
   232→
   233→    // Particle state
   234→    this.particles = [];
   235→
   236→    // Emoji float state
   237→    this.emojiFloats = [];
   238→
   239→    // Speech bubble state
   240→    this.speechBubbles = [];
   241→
   242→    // Status bar text
   243→    this.statusText = '';
   244→
   245→    // Stars (lazy-initialized on first night render)
   246→    this._stars = null;
   247→
   248→    // Ambient particles (fireflies, leaves)
   249→    this._ambientParticles = [];
   250→    this._leafTimer = 0;
   251→    this._waterTiles = null;
   252→    this._windowTiles = null;
   253→    this._lanternPositions = null;
   254→
   255→    // Animation
   256→    this._rafId = null;
   257→    this._lastTime = 0;
   258→    this._renderCallback = null;
   259→  }
   260→
   261→  /** Assign preloaded sprites and bake the tilemap cache. */
   262→  setSprites(sprites) {
   263→    this.tileSprites = sprites.tiles;
   264→    this.objectSprites = sprites.objects;
   265→    this.characterSprites = sprites.characters;
   266→    this.propSprites = sprites.props || null;
   267→    this._bakeTilemapCache();
   268→  }
   269→
   270→  /** Pre-render tilemap to an offscreen canvas for fast blitting. */
   271→  _bakeTilemapCache() {
   272→    const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');
   273→    offscreen.width = MAP_W;
   274→    offscreen.height = MAP_H;
   275→    const octx = offscreen.getContext('2d');
   276→    octx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
   277→
   278→    // Fill with base grass color so no transparency bleeds through
   279→    octx.fillStyle = '#d4c5a9'; // café tile floor base
   280→    octx.fillRect(0, 0, MAP_W, MAP_H);
   281→
   282→    for (let row = 0; row < MAP_ROWS; row++) {
   283→      for (let col = 0; col < MAP_COLS; col++) {
   284→        const tile = MAP[row][col];
   285→        const x = col * TILE_SIZE;
   286→        const y = row * TILE_SIZE;
   287→
   288→        const sprite = this.tileSprites && this.tileSprites.get(tile);
   289→        if (sprite) {
   290→          octx.drawImage(sprite, x, y, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);
   291→        } else {
   292→          octx.fillStyle = TILE_COLORS[tile] || '#ff00ff';
   293→          octx.fillRect(x, y, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);
   294→        }
   295→      }
   296→    }
   297→
   298→    // Bake decorative props on top of tiles (static, never change)
   299→    for (const prop of PROPS) {
   300→      const sprite = this.propSprites && this.propSprites.get(prop.type);
   301→      if (sprite) {
   302→        const pw = (prop.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   303→        const ph = (prop.th || 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   304→        octx.drawImage(sprite, prop.tx * TILE_SIZE, prop.ty * TILE_SIZE, pw, ph);
   305→      }
   306→    }
   307→
   308→    this._tilemapCache = offscreen;
   309→  }
   310→
   311→  _resize() {
   312→    const aspect = MAP_W / MAP_H;
   313→    const winW = window.innerWidth;
   314→    const winH = window.innerHeight;
   315→    const winAspect = winW / winH;
   316→
   317→    let cssW, cssH;
   318→    if (winAspect > aspect) {
   319→      cssH = winH;
   320→      cssW = winH * aspect;
   321→    } else {
   322→      cssW = winW;
   323→      cssH = winW / aspect;
   324→    }
   325→
   326→    this.canvas.style.width = cssW + 'px';
   327→    this.canvas.style.height = cssH + 'px';
   328→    this.canvas.style.margin = 'auto';
   329→
   330→    this.cssScale = cssW / MAP_W;
   331→    this.cssOffsetX = (winW - cssW) / 2;
   332→    this.cssOffsetY = (winH - cssH) / 2;
   333→
   334→    // Resize text overlay to match display resolution
   335→    if (this.textCanvas) {
   336→      const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
   337→      this.textCanvas.style.width = cssW + 'px';
   338→      this.textCanvas.style.height = cssH + 'px';
   339→      this.textCanvas.width = Math.round(cssW * dpr);
   340→      this.textCanvas.height = Math.round(cssH * dpr);
   341→      this.textScale = this.textCanvas.width / MAP_W;
   342→    }
   343→  }
   344→
   345→  // Convert page click coords to tile coords
   346→  pageToTile(pageX, pageY) {
   347→    const rect = this.canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
   348→    const canvasX = (pageX - rect.left) / this.cssScale;
   349→    const canvasY = (pageY - rect.top) / this.cssScale;
   350→    return {
   351→      tx: Math.floor(canvasX / TILE_SIZE),
   352→      ty: Math.floor(canvasY / TILE_SIZE),
   353→      px: canvasX,
   354→      py: canvasY,
   355→    };
   356→  }
   357→
   358→  // ── Tilemap ──
   359→  renderTilemap() {
   360→    if (this._tilemapCache) {
   361→      this.ctx.drawImage(this._tilemapCache, 0, 0);
   362→    } else {
   363→      // Fallback: draw colored rectangles (no sprites loaded yet)
   364→      const ctx = this.ctx;
   365→      for (let row = 0; row < MAP_ROWS; row++) {
   366→        for (let col = 0; col < MAP_COLS; col++) {
   367→          const tile = MAP[row][col];
   368→          ctx.fillStyle = TILE_COLORS[tile] || '#ff00ff';
   369→          ctx.fillRect(col * TILE_SIZE, row * TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);
   370→        }
   371→      }
   372→    }
   373→  }
   374→
   375→  // ── Objects ──
   376→  renderObjects(objects) {
   377→    const ctx = this.ctx;
   378→
   379→    for (const obj of objects) {
   380→      const tx = obj.position.tx;
   381→      const ty = obj.position.ty;
   382→      const pxX = tx * TILE_SIZE;
   383→      const pxY = ty * TILE_SIZE;
   384→      const w = (obj.position.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   385→      const h = (obj.position.th || 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   386→
   387→      const sprite = this.objectSprites && this.objectSprites.get(obj.visual);
   388→
   389→      if (sprite) {
   390→        // Draw sprite scaled to object tile size
   391→        ctx.drawImage(sprite, pxX, pxY, w, h);
   392→      } else {
   393→        // Fallback: colored rectangle
   394→        const color = OBJECT_COLORS[obj.visual] || DEFAULT_OBJ_COLOR;
   395→        ctx.fillStyle = color;
   396→        ctx.fillRect(pxX + 1, pxY + 1, w - 2, h - 2);
   397→        ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';
   398→        ctx.lineWidth = 1;
   399→        ctx.strokeRect(pxX + 0.5, pxY + 0.5, w - 1, h - 1);
   400→      }
   401→
   402→      // Oven flash on interaction (bright overlay for first 200ms)
   403→      if (this._activeInteractions?.has(obj.id) && (obj.id.includes('stove') || obj.id.includes('espresso'))) {
   404→        const elapsed = this._activeInteractions.get(obj.id);
   405→        if (elapsed < 200) {
   406→          ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${0.2 * (1 - elapsed / 200)})`;
   407→          ctx.fillRect(pxX, pxY, w, h);
   408→        }
   409→      }
   410→
   411→      // Spawn particles if object has them
   412→      if (obj.particles && PARTICLE_DEFS[obj.particles]) {
   413→        this._maybeSpawnParticles(obj.particles, pxX + w / 2, pxY);
   414→      }
   415→    }
   416→  }
   417→
   418→  // ── Characters ──
   419→  renderCharacters(characters, debug = false) {
   420→    if (!characters || characters.length === 0) return;
   421→    const ctx = this.ctx;
   422→    const now = performance.now();
   423→
   424→    // Sort by py for depth ordering (lower = drawn on top)
   425→    const sorted = [...characters].sort((a, b) => a.py - b.py);
   426→
   427→    for (const char of sorted) {
   428→      const px = char.px;
   429→      // Idle bob: 1px vertical offset on ~800ms cycle (phase offset per character)
   430→      const idleBob = char.action !== 'walking'
   431→        ? (Math.sin(now * 0.008 + char.tx * 2) > 0 ? 1 : 0)
   432→        : 0;
   433→      const py = char.py + idleBob;
   434→      const sprite = this.characterSprites?.get(char.spriteKey);
   435→
   436→      // Bounce effect on interaction start (scale 1.1→1.0 over 100ms)
   437→      let bounceScale = 1;
   438→      if (char.action === 'interacting') {
   439→        const elapsed = 2000 - char.interactTimer;
   440→        if (elapsed >= 0 && elapsed < 100) {
   441→          bounceScale = 1 + 0.1 * (1 - elapsed / 100);
   442→        }
   443→      }
   444→
   445→      if (sprite) {
   446→        if (char.facing === 'left' || bounceScale !== 1) {
   447→          ctx.save();
   448→          const cx = px + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   449→          const cy = py + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   450→          ctx.translate(cx, cy);
   451→          if (bounceScale !== 1) ctx.scale(bounceScale, bounceScale);
   452→          if (char.facing === 'left') ctx.scale(-1, 1);
   453→          ctx.drawImage(sprite, -TILE_SIZE / 2, -TILE_SIZE / 2, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);
   454→          ctx.restore();
   455→        } else {
   456→          ctx.drawImage(sprite, px, py, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);
   457→        }
   458→      } else {
   459→        // Fallback: simple character shape
   460→        const cx = px + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   461→
   462→        // Body
   463→        ctx.fillStyle = char.colors?.outfit || '#888888';
   464→        ctx.fillRect(cx - 3, py + 6, 6, 8);
   465→
   466→        // Head
   467→        ctx.fillStyle = char.colors?.body || '#ddccbb';
   468→        ctx.beginPath();
   469→        ctx.arc(cx, py + 4, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
   470→        ctx.fill();
   471→
   472→        // Hair
   473→        ctx.fillStyle = char.colors?.hair || '#443322';
   474→        ctx.beginPath();
   475→        ctx.arc(cx, py + 3, 3, Math.PI, Math.PI * 2);
   476→        ctx.fill();
   477→      }
   478→
   479→      // Object-specific interaction particles
   480→      if (char.action === 'interacting') {
   481→        const particleType = getInteractParticleType(char);
   482→        this._maybeSpawnParticles(particleType, px + TILE_SIZE / 2, py + TILE_SIZE / 2);
   483→      }
   484→    }
   485→  }
   486→
   487→  // ── Character labels on text overlay (mood emoji + names) ──
   488→  renderCharacterLabels(characters, debug = false) {
   489→    if (!characters || characters.length === 0) return;
   490→    const ctx = this.textCtx;
   491→    const s = this.textScale;
   492→
   493→    for (const char of characters) {
   494→      const px = char.px * s;
   495→      const py = char.py * s;
   496→      const tileS = TILE_SIZE * s;
   497→
   498→      // Mood emoji above character
   499→      if (char.moodEmoji) {
   500→        ctx.font = `${Math.round(8 * s)}px serif`;
   501→        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
   502→        ctx.fillText(char.moodEmoji, px + tileS / 2, py - 1 * s);
   503→      }
   504→
   505→      // Name label below sprite
   506→      const fontSize = Math.round(5 * s);
   507→      ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;
   508→      ctx.textAlign = 'center';
   509→      const nameX = px + tileS / 2;
   510→      const nameY = py + tileS + 6 * s;
   511→
   512→      const label = debug ? `${char.name} [${char.action}]` : char.name;
   513→      const metrics = ctx.measureText(label);
   514→      const labelW = metrics.width + 3 * s;
   515→
   516→      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.6)';
   517→      ctx.fillRect(nameX - labelW / 2, nameY - 5 * s, labelW, 7 * s);
   518→
   519→      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
   520→      ctx.fillText(label, nameX, nameY);
   521→    }
   522→  }
   523→
   524→  // ── Object labels (debug overlay) ──
   525→  renderObjectLabels(objects) {
   526→    const ctx = this.textCtx;
   527→    const s = this.textScale;
   528→    const fontSize = Math.round(5 * s);
   529→    ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;
   530→    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
   531→
   532→    for (const obj of objects) {
   533→      const tx = obj.position.tx;
   534→      const ty = obj.position.ty;
   535→      const pxX = (tx * TILE_SIZE + ((obj.position.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE) / 2) * s;
   536→      const pxY = (ty * TILE_SIZE - 2) * s;
   537→
   538→      const text = `${obj.name} [${obj.state}]`;
   539→      const metrics = ctx.measureText(text);
   540→      const textW = metrics.width + 4 * s;
   541→
   542→      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)';
   543→      ctx.fillRect(pxX - textW / 2, pxY - 5 * s, textW, 7 * s);
   544→
   545→      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
   546→      ctx.fillText(text, pxX, pxY);
   547→
   548→      // Timer bar under object
   549→      if (obj.autoNextDuration !== null) {
   550→        const remaining = obj.timeRemainingMs;
   551→        const total = obj.autoNextDuration;
   552→        const pct = (total - remaining) / total;
   553→        const barW = ((obj.position.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE - 4) * s;
   554→        const barY = ((ty + (obj.position.th || 1)) * TILE_SIZE + 1) * s;
   555→        const barX = (tx * TILE_SIZE + 2) * s;
   556→
   557→        ctx.fillStyle = '#333333';
   558→        ctx.fillRect(barX, barY, barW, 2 * s);
   559→        ctx.fillStyle = pct > 0.85 ? '#d04020' : pct > 0.66 ? '#d0a020' : '#40a040';
   560→        ctx.fillRect(barX, barY, barW * pct, 2 * s);
   561→      }
   562→    }
   563→  }
   564→
   565→  // ── Particles ──
   566→  _maybeSpawnParticles(type, x, y) {
   567→    const def = PARTICLE_DEFS[type];
   568→    if (!def) return;
   569→    const active = this.particles.filter(p => p.type === type).length;
   570→    if (active >= def.count * 2) return;
   571→
   572→    for (let i = 0; i < def.count; i++) {
   573→      const color = def.colors
   574→        ? def.colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * def.colors.length)]
   575→        : def.color;
   576→
   577→      let vx, vy;
   578→      if (def.dir === 'down') {
   579→        vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
   580→        vy = def.speed + Math.random() * 0.2;
   581→      } else if (def.dir === 'radial') {
   582→        const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
   583→        vx = Math.cos(angle) * def.speed;
   584→        vy = Math.sin(angle) * def.speed;
   585→      } else {
   586→        vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
   587→        vy = -def.speed - Math.random() * 0.2;
   588→      }
   589→
   590→      this.particles.push({
   591→        type,
   592→        x: x + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 8,
   593→        y: y,
   594→        vx,
   595→        vy,
   596→        life: def.life * (0.7 + Math.random() * 0.6),
   597→        maxLife: def.life,
   598→        color,
   599→        size: def.size,
   600→        shape: def.shape || 'circle',
   601→        wobble: def.wobble || false,
   602→        phase: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,
   603→        age: 0,
   604→      });
   605→    }
   606→  }
   607→
   608→  renderParticles(dt) {
   609→    const ctx = this.ctx;
   610→
   611→    for (let i = this.particles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   612→      const p = this.particles[i];
   613→      p.life -= dt;
   614→      if (p.life <= 0) {
   615→        this.particles.splice(i, 1);
   616→        continue;
   617→      }
   618→
   619→      p.x += p.vx;
   620→      p.y += p.vy;
   621→      p.age = (p.age || 0) + dt;
   622→
   623→      const alpha = Math.max(0, p.life / p.maxLife);
   624→      ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
   625→      ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
   626→
   627→      // Sine wave wobble for steam/smoke
   628→      const drawX = p.wobble
   629→        ? p.x + Math.sin(p.age * 0.006 + (p.phase || 0)) * 1.5
   630→        : p.x;
   631→
   632→      if (p.shape === 'square') {
   633→        ctx.fillRect(drawX - p.size / 2, p.y - p.size / 2, p.size, p.size);
   634→      } else {
   635→        ctx.beginPath();
   636→        ctx.arc(drawX, p.y, p.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
   637→        ctx.fill();
   638→      }
   639→    }
   640→
   641→    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
   642→  }
   643→
   644→  // ── Speech Bubble ──
   645→  addSpeechBubble(tx, ty, text, durationMs = 3000) {
   646→    this.speechBubbles.push({
   647→      x: tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2,
   648→      y: ty * TILE_SIZE - 10,
   649→      text,
   650→      life: durationMs,
   651→      maxLife: durationMs,
   652→    });
   653→  }
   654→
   655→  /** Add a speech bubble attached to a character (follows their position). */
   656→  addCharacterSpeech(character, text, durationMs = 5000) {
   657→    // Remove any existing bubble for this character
   658→    this.speechBubbles = this.speechBubbles.filter(b => b.character !== character);
   659→
   660→    // Truncate long text for the tiny canvas
   661→    const maxLen = 60;
   662→    const truncated = text.length > maxLen ? text.substring(0, maxLen - 1) + '\u2026' : text;
   663→
   664→    this.speechBubbles.push({
   665→      character,
   666→      text: truncated,
   667→      life: durationMs,
   668→      maxLife: durationMs,
   669→    });
   670→  }
   671→
   672→  setStatus(text) {
   673→    this.statusText = text;
   674→  }
   675→
   676→  _wrapText(ctx, text, maxWidth) {
   677→    const words = text.split(' ');
   678→    const lines = [];
   679→    let current = '';
   680→
   681→    for (const word of words) {
   682→      const test = current ? current + ' ' + word : word;
   683→      if (ctx.measureText(test).width > maxWidth && current) {
   684→        lines.push(current);
   685→        current = word;
   686→      } else {
   687→        current = test;
   688→      }
   689→    }
   690→    if (current) lines.push(current);
   691→    return lines.length > 0 ? lines : [text];
   692→  }
   693→
   694→  renderSpeechBubbles(dt) {
   695→    const ctx = this.textCtx;
   696→    const s = this.textScale;
   697→    const fontSize = Math.round(5 * s);
   698→    ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;
   699→    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
   700→
   701→    for (let i = this.speechBubbles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   702→      const b = this.speechBubbles[i];
   703→      b.life -= dt;
   704→      if (b.life <= 0) {
   705→        this.speechBubbles.splice(i, 1);
   706→        continue;
   707→      }
   708→
   709→      // Calculate anchor position (native coords scaled to text canvas)
   710→      let anchorX, anchorY;
   711→      if (b.character) {
   712→        anchorX = (b.character.px + TILE_SIZE / 2) * s;
   713→        anchorY = (b.character.py - 10) * s;
   714→      } else {
   715→        anchorX = b.x * s;
   716→        anchorY = b.y * s;
   717→      }
   718→
   719→      const alpha = Math.min(1, b.life / 500);
   720→      ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
   721→
   722→      // Word wrap
   723→      const maxBubbleW = 100 * s;
   724→      const lines = this._wrapText(ctx, b.text, maxBubbleW - 8 * s);
   725→      const lineH = 7 * s;
   726→      const padX = 4 * s;
   727→      const padY = 3 * s;
   728→
   729→      let maxLineW = 0;
   730→      for (const line of lines) {
   731→        const w = ctx.measureText(line).width;
   732→        if (w > maxLineW) maxLineW = w;
   733→      }
   734→
   735→      const bw = maxLineW + padX * 2;
   736→      const bh = lines.length * lineH + padY * 2;
   737→      let bx = anchorX - bw / 2;
   738→      const by = anchorY - bh;
   739→
   740→      // Clamp to canvas bounds
   741→      bx = Math.max(s, Math.min(bx, this.textCanvas.width - bw - s));
   742→
   743→      // Background
   744→      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
   745→      ctx.beginPath();
   746→      ctx.roundRect(bx, by, bw, bh, 3 * s);
   747→      ctx.fill();
   748→
   749→      // Tail
   750→      const tailX = Math.max(bx + 4 * s, Math.min(anchorX, bx + bw - 4 * s));
   751→      ctx.beginPath();
   752→      ctx.moveTo(tailX - 3 * s, by + bh);
   753→      ctx.lineTo(tailX, by + bh + 4 * s);
   754→      ctx.lineTo(tailX + 3 * s, by + bh);
   755→      ctx.fill();
   756→
   757→      // Text lines
   758→      ctx.fillStyle = '#222222';
   759→      for (let l = 0; l < lines.length; l++) {
   760→        ctx.fillText(lines[l], bx + bw / 2, by + padY + (l + 1) * lineH - s);
   761→      }
   762→    }
   763→
   764→    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
   765→  }
   766→
   767→  // ── Status Bar ──
   768→  renderStatusBar() {
   769→    if (!this.statusText) return;
   770→
   771→    const ctx = this.textCtx;
   772→    const s = this.textScale;
   773→    const tw = this.textCanvas.width;
   774→    const th = this.textCanvas.height;
   775→    const barH = 12 * s;
   776→    const y = th - barH;
   777→
   778→    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.7)';
   779→    ctx.fillRect(0, y, tw, barH);
   780→
   781→    const fontSize = Math.round(5 * s);
   782→    ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;
   783→    ctx.fillStyle = '#d0ccc4';
   784→    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
   785→
   786→    // Truncate if too wide
   787→    let text = this.statusText;
   788→    while (ctx.measureText(text).width > tw - 8 * s && text.length > 10) {
   789→      text = text.substring(0, text.length - 4) + '\u2026';
   790→    }
   791→
   792→    ctx.fillText(text, tw / 2, y + 8 * s);
   793→  }
   794→
   795→  // ── Emoji Float ──
   796→  addEmojiFloat(tx, ty, emoji) {
   797→    this.emojiFloats.push({
   798→      x: tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2,
   799→      y: ty * TILE_SIZE,
   800→      emoji,
   801→      life: 1500,
   802→      maxLife: 1500,
   803→    });
   804→  }
   805→
   806→  renderEmojiFloats(dt) {
   807→    const ctx = this.textCtx;
   808→    const s = this.textScale;
   809→    ctx.font = `${Math.round(12 * s)}px serif`;
   810→    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
   811→
   812→    for (let i = this.emojiFloats.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   813→      const e = this.emojiFloats[i];
   814→      e.life -= dt;
   815→      if (e.life <= 0) {
   816→        this.emojiFloats.splice(i, 1);
   817→        continue;
   818→      }
   819→
   820→      const progress = 1 - e.life / e.maxLife;
   821→      const alpha = 1 - progress;
   822→      const yOff = -progress * 20;
   823→
   824→      ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
   825→      ctx.fillText(e.emoji, e.x * s, (e.y + yOff) * s);
   826→    }
   827→
   828→    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
   829→  }
   830→
   831→  // ── Highlight a tile (for hover/click feedback) ──
   832→  highlightTile(tx, ty, color = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)') {

   835→  }
   836→
   837→  // ── Day/Night Cycle ──
   838→
   839→  _initStars() {
   840→    this._stars = [];
   841→    for (let row = 0; row < MAP_ROWS; row++) {
   842→      for (let col = 0; col < MAP_COLS; col++) {
   843→        const tile = MAP[row][col];
   844→        if (tile === T.WALL || tile === T.DOOR) {
   845→          const count = 1 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 2);
   846→          for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   847→            this._stars.push({
   848→              x: col * TILE_SIZE + Math.random() * TILE_SIZE,
   849→              y: row * TILE_SIZE + Math.random() * TILE_SIZE,
   850→              phase: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,
   851→              size: 0.5 + Math.random() * 0.8,
   852→            });
   853→          }
   854→        }
   855→      }
   856→    }
   857→  }
   858→
   859→  _initWaterTiles() {
   860→    this._waterTiles = [];
   861→    for (let row = 0; row < MAP_ROWS; row++) {
   862→      for (let col = 0; col < MAP_COLS; col++) {
   863→        if (false) { // no water tiles in café
   864→          this._waterTiles.push({
   865→            x: col * TILE_SIZE,
   866→            y: row * TILE_SIZE,
   867→            phase: (row * MAP_COLS + col) * 0.7,
   868→          });
   869→        }
   870→      }
   871→    }
   872→  }
   873→
   874→  _initWindowTiles() {
   875→    this._windowTiles = [];
   876→    for (let row = 0; row < MAP_ROWS; row++) {
   877→      for (let col = 0; col < MAP_COLS; col++) {
   878→        if (MAP[row][col] === T.FLOOR_WOOD || MAP[row][col] === T.FLOOR_TILE) {
   879→          const neighbors = [
   880→            [row - 1, col], [row + 1, col], [row, col - 1], [row, col + 1],
   881→          ];
   882→          const hasWall = neighbors.some(([r, c]) =>
   883→            r >= 0 && r < MAP_ROWS && c >= 0 && c < MAP_COLS && MAP[r][c] === T.WALL
   884→          );
   885→          if (hasWall) {
   886→            this._windowTiles.push({ x: col * TILE_SIZE, y: row * TILE_SIZE });
   887→          }
   888→        }
   889→      }
   890→    }
   891→  }
   892→
   893→  _initLanternPositions() {
   894→    this._lanternPositions = [];
   895→    for (const prop of PROPS) {
   896→      if (prop.type === 'lantern') {
   897→        this._lanternPositions.push({
   898→          cx: prop.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2,
   899→          cy: prop.ty * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2,
   900→        });
   901→      }
   902→    }
   903→  }
   904→
   905→  _getDayNightState(minuteOfDay) {
   906→    const m = minuteOfDay;
   907→    const TRANS = 30;
   908→    const half = TRANS / 2;
   909→
   910→    const NIGHT   = [0, 0, 50, 0.3];
   911→    const GOLDEN  = [255, 160, 40, 0.08];
   912→    const MORNING = [255, 200, 50, 0.1];
   913→    const DAY     = [0, 0, 0, 0];
   914→    const EVENING = [255, 100, 0, 0.15];
   915→
   916→    function lerp4(a, b, t) {
   917→      return [
   918→        a[0] + (b[0] - a[0]) * t,
   919→        a[1] + (b[1] - a[1]) * t,
   920→        a[2] + (b[2] - a[2]) * t,
   921→        a[3] + (b[3] - a[3]) * t,
   922→      ];
   923→    }
   924→
   925→    function lerpN(a, b, t) { return a + (b - a) * t; }
   926→
   927→    // Pre-dawn golden hour at 5am (300), sunrise at 6am (360)
   928→    if (m < 300 - half) return { tint: NIGHT, nightFactor: 1 };
   929→    if (m < 300 + half) {
   930→      const t = (m - (300 - half)) / TRANS;
   931→      return { tint: lerp4(NIGHT, GOLDEN, t), nightFactor: lerpN(1, 0.15, t) };
   932→    }
   933→    if (m < 360 - half) return { tint: GOLDEN, nightFactor: 0.15 };
   934→    if (m < 360 + half) {
   935→      const t = (m - (360 - half)) / TRANS;
   936→      return { tint: lerp4(GOLDEN, MORNING, t), nightFactor: lerpN(0.15, 0, t) };
   937→    }
   938→    // Morning (6-10am)
   939→    if (m < 600 - half) return { tint: MORNING, nightFactor: 0 };
   940→    if (m < 600 + half) {
   941→      const t = (m - (600 - half)) / TRANS;
   942→      return { tint: lerp4(MORNING, DAY, t), nightFactor: 0 };
   943→    }
   944→    // Day (10am-5pm)
   945→    if (m < 1020 - half) return { tint: DAY, nightFactor: 0 };
   946→    if (m < 1020 + half) {
   947→      const t = (m - (1020 - half)) / TRANS;
   948→      return { tint: lerp4(DAY, EVENING, t), nightFactor: 0 };
   949→    }
   950→    // Evening (5-7pm)
   951→    if (m < 1140 - half) return { tint: EVENING, nightFactor: 0 };
   952→    // Sunset golden hour at 7pm (1140), night at 8pm (1200)
   953→    if (m < 1140 + half) {
   954→      const t = (m - (1140 - half)) / TRANS;
   955→      return { tint: lerp4(EVENING, GOLDEN, t), nightFactor: lerpN(0, 0.15, t) };
   956→    }
   957→    if (m < 1200 - half) return { tint: GOLDEN, nightFactor: 0.15 };
   958→    if (m < 1200 + half) {
   959→      const t = (m - (1200 - half)) / TRANS;
   960→      return { tint: lerp4(GOLDEN, NIGHT, t), nightFactor: lerpN(0.15, 1, t) };
   961→    }
   962→    return { tint: NIGHT, nightFactor: 1 };
   963→  }
   964→
   965→  renderDayNightCycle(minuteOfDay, now) {
   966→    const { tint, nightFactor } = this._getDayNightState(minuteOfDay);
   967→    const ctx = this.ctx;
   968→
   969→    // Tint overlay — one fillRect per frame
   970→    if (tint[3] > 0) {
   971→      ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${tint[0] | 0}, ${tint[1] | 0}, ${tint[2] | 0}, ${tint[3]})`;
   972→      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, MAP_W, MAP_H);
   973→    }
   974→
   975→    // Window glow — warm amber rectangles on interior tiles at night
   976→    if (nightFactor > 0.1) {
   977→      if (!this._windowTiles) this._initWindowTiles();
   978→      ctx.fillStyle = '#f0d888';
   979→      ctx.globalAlpha = 0.15 + nightFactor * 0.1;
   980→      for (const tile of this._windowTiles) {
   981→        ctx.fillRect(tile.x, tile.y, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);
   982→      }
   983→      ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
   984→    }
   985→
   986→    // Lantern glow — radial gradient circles at lantern positions
   987→    if (nightFactor > 0.1) {
   988→      if (!this._lanternPositions) this._initLanternPositions();
   989→      const glowAlpha = 0.3 + nightFactor * 0.2;
   990→      const radius = TILE_SIZE * 2;
   991→
   992→      for (const lantern of this._lanternPositions) {
   993→        const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(
   994→          lantern.cx, lantern.cy, 0,
   995→          lantern.cx, lantern.cy, radius
   996→        );
   997→        gradient.addColorStop(0, `rgba(240, 216, 136, ${glowAlpha})`);
   998→        gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(240, 216, 136, 0)');
   999→        ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
  1000→        ctx.fillRect(
  1001→          lantern.cx - radius, lantern.cy - radius,
  1002→          radius * 2, radius * 2
  1003→        );
  1004→      }
  1005→    }
  1006→
  1007→    // Stars — twinkling white dots on WALL/DOOR tiles during night
  1008→    if (nightFactor > 0) {
  1009→      if (!this._stars) this._initStars();
  1010→      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
  1011→      for (const star of this._stars) {
  1012→        const twinkle = 0.3 + 0.7 * (0.5 + 0.5 * Math.sin(now * 0.003 + star.phase));
  1013→        ctx.globalAlpha = nightFactor * twinkle;
  1014→        ctx.fillRect(star.x - star.size / 2, star.y - star.size / 2, star.size, star.size);
  1015→      }
  1016→      ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
  1017→    }
  1018→  }
  1019→
  1020→  // ── Pond Ripple ──
  1021→  renderPondRipple(now) {
  1022→    if (!this._waterTiles) this._initWaterTiles();
  1023→    const ctx = this.ctx;
  1024→    for (const tile of this._waterTiles) {
  1025→      const shimmer = 0.5 + 0.5 * Math.sin(now * 0.002 + tile.phase);
  1026→      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
  1027→      ctx.globalAlpha = shimmer * 0.1;
  1028→      ctx.fillRect(tile.x, tile.y, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);
  1029→    }
  1030→    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
  1031→  }
  1032→
  1033→  // ── Ambient Particles (fireflies, leaves) ──
  1034→  _updateAmbientParticles(dt, minuteOfDay) {
  1035→    const isNight = minuteOfDay >= 1200 || minuteOfDay < 360;
  1036→
  1037→    // Fireflies — night only, up to 6
  1038→    if (isNight) {
  1039→      const fireflyCount = this._ambientParticles.filter(p => p.type === 'firefly').length;
  1040→      if (fireflyCount < 6) {
  1041→        this._ambientParticles.push({
  1042→          type: 'firefly',
  1043→          x: Math.random() * MAP_W,
  1044→          y: MAP_H * 0.2 + Math.random() * MAP_H * 0.6,
  1045→          vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.02,
  1046→          vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.02,
  1047→          dirTimer: 1000 + Math.random() * 2000,
  1048→          phase: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,
  1049→          size: 1 + Math.random() * 0.5,
  1050→          life: 8000 + Math.random() * 12000,
  1051→        });
  1052→      }
  1053→    }
  1054→
  1055→    // Leaf — one every 15-30 seconds
  1056→    this._leafTimer -= dt;
  1057→    if (this._leafTimer <= 0) {
  1058→      this._leafTimer = 15000 + Math.random() * 15000;
  1059→      const hasLeaf = this._ambientParticles.some(p => p.type === 'leaf');
  1060→      if (!hasLeaf) {
  1061→        this._ambientParticles.push({
  1062→          type: 'leaf',
  1063→          x: -4,
  1064→          y: Math.random() * MAP_H * 0.3,
  1065→          vx: 0.015 + Math.random() * 0.01,
  1066→          vy: 0.01 + Math.random() * 0.008,
  1067→          rotation: Math.random() * Math.PI,
  1068→          rotSpeed: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.002,
  1069→          life: 30000,
  1070→          color: Math.random() > 0.5 ? '#5a7a3a' : '#7a5a2a',
  1071→        });
  1072→      }
  1073→    }
  1074→
  1075→    // Update all ambient particles
  1076→    for (let i = this._ambientParticles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  1077→      const p = this._ambientParticles[i];
  1078→      p.life -= dt;
  1079→
  1080→      if (p.type === 'firefly') {
  1081→        if (!isNight) p.life = Math.min(p.life, 500); // fade out at dawn
  1082→        p.dirTimer -= dt;
  1083→        if (p.dirTimer <= 0) {
  1084→          p.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.02;
  1085→          p.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.02;
  1086→          p.dirTimer = 1000 + Math.random() * 2000;
  1087→        }
  1088→        if (p.x < 10 || p.x > MAP_W - 10) p.vx = -p.vx;
  1089→        if (p.y < 10 || p.y > MAP_H - 20) p.vy = -p.vy;
  1090→      }
  1091→
  1092→      p.x += p.vx * dt;
  1093→      p.y += p.vy * dt;
  1094→      if (p.rotation !== undefined) p.rotation += p.rotSpeed * dt;
  1095→
  1096→      if (p.life <= 0 || p.x > MAP_W + 10 || p.y > MAP_H + 10) {
  1097→        this._ambientParticles.splice(i, 1);
  1098→      }
  1099→    }
  1100→  }
  1101→
  1102→  renderAmbientParticles(now) {
  1103→    const ctx = this.ctx;
  1104→
  1105→    for (const p of this._ambientParticles) {
  1106→      if (p.type === 'firefly') {
  1107→        const glow = 0.4 + 0.6 * (0.5 + 0.5 * Math.sin(now * 0.004 + p.phase));
  1108→        const fade = Math.min(1, p.life / 500);
  1109→        ctx.globalAlpha = glow * fade;
  1110→        ctx.fillStyle = '#aadd44';
  1111→        ctx.beginPath();
  1112→        ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  1113→        ctx.fill();
  1114→        // Glow halo
  1115→        ctx.globalAlpha = glow * fade * 0.25;
  1116→        ctx.beginPath();
  1117→        ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.size * 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  1118→        ctx.fill();
  1119→      } else if (p.type === 'leaf') {
  1120→        ctx.globalAlpha = 0.7;
  1121→        ctx.save();
  1122→        ctx.translate(p.x, p.y);
  1123→        ctx.rotate(p.rotation);
  1124→        ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
  1125→        ctx.fillRect(-1.5, -1, 3, 2);
  1126→        ctx.restore();
  1127→      }
  1128→    }
  1129→
  1130→    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
  1131→  }
  1132→
  1133→  // ── Full render frame ──
  1134→  startLoop(getObjects, getCharacters, options = {}) {
  1135→    this._lastTime = performance.now();
  1136→
  1137→    const frame = (now) => {
  1138→      const dt = Math.min(now - this._lastTime, 100);
  1139→      this._lastTime = now;
  1140→
  1141→      const objects = getObjects();
  1142→      const characters = getCharacters ? getCharacters() : null;
  1143→      const showDebug = options.showDebug && options.showDebug();
  1144→
  1145→      // Build active interactions map for object flash effects
  1146→      this._activeInteractions = null;
  1147→      if (characters) {
  1148→        for (const char of characters) {
  1149→          if (char.action === 'interacting' && char.targetObjectId) {
  1150→            if (!this._activeInteractions) this._activeInteractions = new Map();
  1151→            this._activeInteractions.set(char.targetObjectId, 2000 - char.interactTimer);
  1152→          }
  1153→        }
  1154→      }
  1155→
  1156→      // ── Main canvas (pixel art at native 768×1152 resolution) ──
  1157→      // Fill with solid background to prevent transparency bleed-through
  1158→      this.ctx.fillStyle = '#1a1a2e'; // café night background
  1159→      this.ctx.fillRect(0, 0, MAP_W, MAP_H);
  1160→
  1161→      // Layer 1: tilemap
  1162→      this.renderTilemap();
  1163→
  1164→      // Layer 1.5: pond ripple (water tile oscillation)
  1165→      this.renderPondRipple(now);
  1166→
  1167→      // Layer 2: objects
  1168→      this.renderObjects(objects);
  1169→
  1170→      // Layer 3: characters (sprites only, labels on text canvas)
  1171→      if (characters) {
  1172→        this.renderCharacters(characters);
  1173→      }
  1174→
  1175→      // Layer 4: particles
  1176→      this.renderParticles(dt);
  1177→
  1178→      // Layer 5: day/night cycle tint + stars
  1179→      if (options.getSimClock) {
  1180→        const clock = options.getSimClock();
  1181→        this.renderDayNightCycle(clock.minuteOfDay, now);
  1182→        this._updateAmbientParticles(dt, clock.minuteOfDay);
  1183→      }
  1184→
  1185→      // Layer 5.5: ambient particles (fireflies glow through night tint, leaves)
  1186→      this.renderAmbientParticles(now);
  1187→
  1188→      // ── Text overlay canvas (high-res for crisp text/emoji) ──
  1189→      this.textCtx.clearRect(0, 0, this.textCanvas.width, this.textCanvas.height);
  1190→
  1191→      // Character labels (mood emoji + names)
  1192→      if (characters) {
  1193→        this.renderCharacterLabels(characters, showDebug);
  1194→      }
  1195→
  1196→      // Emoji floats
  1197→      this.renderEmojiFloats(dt);
  1198→
  1199→      // Speech bubbles
  1200→      this.renderSpeechBubbles(dt);
  1201→
  1202→      // Status bar
  1203→      this.renderStatusBar();
  1204→
  1205→      // Debug object labels
  1206→      if (showDebug) {
  1207→        this.renderObjectLabels(objects);
  1208→      }
  1209→
  1210→      // Custom render callback
  1211→      if (this._renderCallback) {
  1212→        this._renderCallback(this.ctx, dt);
  1213→      }
  1214→
  1215→      this._rafId = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
  1216→    };
  1217→
  1218→    this._rafId = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
  1219→  }
  1220→
  1221→  stopLoop() {
  1222→    if (this._rafId) {
  1223→      cancelAnimationFrame(this._rafId);
  1224→      this._rafId = null;
  1225→    }
  1226→  }
  1227→
  1228→  onRender(callback) {
  1229→    this._renderCallback = callback;
  1230→  }
  1231→}
  1232→

156\u2192\n   157\u2192  const promises = [];\n   158\u2192\n   159\u2192  // Tile sprites\n   160\u2192  for (const [tileId, path] of Object.entries(TILE_SPRITES)) {\n   161\u2192    promises.push(\n    // Particle state\n   234\u2192    this.particles = [];\n   235\u2192\n   236\u2192    // Emoji float state\n   237\u2192    this.emojiFloats = [];\n   238\u2192\n   239\u2192    // Speech bubble Pre-render tilemap to an offscreen canvas for fast blitting. */\n   271\u2192  _bakeTilemapCache() {\n   272\u2192    const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');\n   273\u2192    offscreen.width = MAP_W;\n   274\u2192    offscreen.height = MAP_H;\n   275\u2192    const octx = offscreen.getContext('2d');\n   276\u2192    octx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;\n   277\u2192\n   278\u2192    // Fill with base grass color so no transparency bleeds through\n   279\u2192    octx.fillStyle = '#d4c5a9'; // caf\u00e9 tile floor base\n   280\u2192    octx.fillRect(0, 0, MAP_W, MAP_H);\n   281\u2192\n   282\u2192    for (let row = 0; row < MAP_ROWS; row++) {\n   283\u2192      for (let col = 0; col < MAP_COLS; col++) {\n   284\u2192        const tile = MAP[row][col];\n   285\u2192        const x = col * TILE_SIZE;\n   286\u2192        const y = row * TILE_SIZE;\n   287\u2192\n   288\u2192        const sprite = this.tileSprites && this.tileSprites.get(tile);\n   289\u2192        if (sprite) {\n   290\u2192          octx.drawImage(sprite, x, y, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);\n   291\u2192        } else {\n   292\u2192          octx.fillStyle = TILE_COLORS[tile] || top of tiles (static, never change)\n   299\u2192    for (const prop of PROPS) {\n   300\u2192      const sprite = this.propSprites && this.propSprites.get(prop.type);\n   301\u2192      if (sprite) {\n   302\u2192        const pw = (prop.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE;\n   303\u2192        const ph = (prop.th || 1) * TILE_SIZE;\n   304\u2192        octx.drawImage(sprite, prop.tx * TILE_SIZE, prop.ty * TILE_SIZE, pw, ph);\n   305\u2192      }\n   306\u2192    }\n   307\u2192\n   308\u2192    this._tilemapCache = offscreen;\n   309\u2192  }\n   310\u2192\n   311\u2192  _resize() {\n   312\u2192    const aspect = MAP_W / MAP_H;\n   313\u2192    const winW = window.innerWidth;\n   314\u2192    const winH = window.innerHeight;\n   315\u2192    const winAspect = winW / winH;\n   316\u2192\n   317\u2192    let cssW, cssH;\n   318\u2192    if (winAspect > aspect) {\n   319\u2192      cssH = winH;\n   320\u2192      cssW = winH * aspect;\n   321\u2192    } else {\n   322\u2192      cssW = winW;\n   323\u2192      cssH = winW / aspect;\n   324\u2192    }\n   325\u2192\n   326\u2192    this.canvas.style.width = cssW + 'px';\n   327\u2192    this.canvas.style.height = cssH + 'px';\n   328\u2192    this.canvas.style.margin = 'auto';\n   329\u2192\n   330\u2192    this.cssScale = cssW / MAP_W;\n   331\u2192    this.cssOffsetX = (winW - cssW) / 2;\n   332\u2192    this.cssOffsetY = (winH - cssH) / 2;\n   333\u2192\n   334\u2192    // Resize text overlay to match display resolution\n   335\u2192    if (this.textCanvas) {\n   336\u2192      const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;\n   337\u2192      this.textCanvas.style.width = cssW + 'px';\n   338\u2192      this.textCanvas.style.height = cssH + 'px';\n   339\u2192      this.textCanvas.width = Math.round(cssW * dpr);\n   340\u2192      this.textCanvas.height = Math.round(cssH * dpr);\n   341\u2192      this.textScale = this.textCanvas.width / MAP_W;\n   342\u2192    }\n   343\u2192  }\n   344\u2192\n   345\u2192  // Convert page click coords to tile coords\n   346\u2192  pageToTile(pageX, pageY) {\n   347\u2192    const rect = this.canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\n   348\u2192    const canvasX = (pageX - rect.left) / this.cssScale;\n   349\u2192    const canvasY = (pageY - rect.top) / this.cssScale;\n   350\u2192    return {\n   351\u2192      tx: Math.floor(canvasX / TILE_SIZE),\n   352\u2192      ty: Math.floor(canvasY / TILE_SIZE),\n   353\u2192      px: canvasX,\n   354\u2192      py: canvasY,\n   355\u2192    };\n   356\u2192  }\n   357\u2192\n   358\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Tilemap \u2500\u2500\n   359\u2192  renderTilemap() {\n   360\u2192    if (this._tilemapCache) {\n   361\u2192      this.ctx.drawImage(this._tilemapCache, 0, 0);\n   362\u2192    } else {\n   363\u2192      // Fallback: draw colored rectangles (no sprites loaded yet)\n   364\u2192      const ctx = this.ctx;\n   365\u2192      for (let row = 0; row < MAP_ROWS; row++) {\n   366\u2192        for (let col = 0; col < MAP_COLS; col++) {\n   367\u2192          const tile = MAP[row][col];\n   368\u2192          ctx.fillStyle = TILE_COLORS[tile] || '#ff00ff';\n   369\u2192          ctx.fillRect(col * TILE_SIZE, row * TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);\n   370\u2192        }\n   371\u2192      }\n   372\u2192    }\n   373\u2192  }\n   374\u2192\n   375\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Objects \u2500\u2500\n   376\u2192  renderObjects(objects) {\n   377\u2192    const ctx = this.ctx;\n   378\u2192\n   379\u2192    for (const obj of objects) {\n   380\u2192      const tx = obj.position.tx;\n   381\u2192      const ty = obj.position.ty;\n   382\u2192      const pxX = tx * TILE_SIZE;\n   383\u2192      const pxY = ty * TILE_SIZE;\n   384\u2192      const w = (obj.position.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE;\n   385\u2192      const h = (obj.position.th || 1) * TILE_SIZE;\n   386\u2192\n   387\u2192      const sprite = this.objectSprites && this.objectSprites.get(obj.visual);\n   388\u2192\n   389\u2192      if (sprite) {\n   390\u2192        // Draw sprite scaled to object tile size\n   391\u2192        ctx.drawImage(sprite, pxX, pxY, w, h);\n   392\u2192      } else {\n   393\u2192        // Fallback: colored rectangle\n   394\u2192        const color = OBJECT_COLORS[obj.visual] || DEFAULT_OBJ_COLOR;\n   395\u2192        ctx.fillStyle = color;\n   396\u2192        ctx.fillRect(pxX + 1, pxY + 1, w - 2, h - 2);\n   397\u2192        ctx.strokeStyle = '#000000';\n   398\u2192        ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n   399\u2192        ctx.strokeRect(pxX + 0.5, pxY + 0.5, w - 1, h - 1);\n   400\u2192      }\n   401\u2192\n   402\u2192      // Oven flash on interaction (bright overlay for first 200ms)\n   403\u2192      if (this._activeInteractions?.has(obj.id) && (obj.id.includes('stove') || obj.id.includes('espresso'))) {\n   404\u2192        const elapsed = this._activeInteractions.get(obj.id);\n   405\u2192        if (elapsed < 200) {\n   406\u2192          ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${0.2 * (1 - elapsed / 200)})`;\n   407\u2192          ctx.fillRect(pxX, pxY, w, h);\n   408\u2192        }\n   409\u2192      }\n   410\u2192\n   411\u2192      // Spawn particles if object has them\n   412\u2192      if (obj.particles && PARTICLE_DEFS[obj.particles]) {\n   413\u2192        this._maybeSpawnParticles(obj.particles, pxX + w / 2, pxY);\n   414\u2192      }\n   415\u2192    }\n   416\u2192  }\n   417\u2192\n   418\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Characters \u2500\u2500\n   419\u2192  renderCharacters(characters, debug = false) {\n   420\u2192    if (!characters || characters.length === 0) return;\n   421\u2192    const ctx = this.ctx;\n   422\u2192    const now = performance.now();\n   423\u2192\n   424\u2192    // Sort by py for depth ordering (lower = drawn on top)\n   425\u2192    const sorted = [...characters].sort((a, b) => a.py - b.py);\n   426\u2192\n   427\u2192    for (const char of sorted) {\n   428\u2192      const px = char.px;\n   429\u2192      // Idle bob: 1px vertical offset on ~800ms cycle (phase offset per character)\n   430\u2192      const idleBob = char.action !== 'walking'\n   431\u2192        ? (Math.sin(now * 0.008 + char.tx * 2) > 0 ? 1 : 0)\n   432\u2192        : 0;\n   433\u2192      const py = char.py + idleBob;\n   434\u2192      const sprite = this.characterSprites?.get(char.spriteKey);\n   435\u2192\n   436\u2192      // Bounce effect on interaction start (scale 1.1\u21921.0 over 100ms)\n   437\u2192      let bounceScale = 1;\n   438\u2192      if (char.action === 'interacting') {\n   439\u2192        const elapsed = 2000 - char.interactTimer;\n   440\u2192        if (elapsed >= 0 && elapsed < 100) {\n   441\u2192          bounceScale = 1 + 0.1 * (1 - elapsed / 100);\n   442\u2192        }\n   443\u2192      }\n   444\u2192\n   445\u2192      if (sprite) {\n   446\u2192        if (char.facing === 'left' || bounceScale !== 1) {\n   447\u2192          ctx.save();\n   448\u2192          const cx = px + TILE_SIZE / 2;\n   449\u2192          const cy = py + TILE_SIZE / 2;\n   450\u2192          ctx.translate(cx, cy);\n   451\u2192          if (bounceScale !== 1) ctx.scale(bounceScale, bounceScale);\n   452\u2192          if (char.facing === 'left') ctx.scale(-1, 1);\n   453\u2192          ctx.drawImage(sprite, -TILE_SIZE / 2, -TILE_SIZE / 2, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);\n   454\u2192          ctx.restore();\n   455\u2192        } else {\n   456\u2192          ctx.drawImage(sprite, px, py, TILE_SIZE, TILE_SIZE);\n   457\u2192        }\n   458\u2192      } else {\n   459\u2192        // Fallback: simple character shape\n   460\u2192        const cx = px + TILE_SIZE / 2;\n   461\u2192\n   462\u2192        // Body\n   463\u2192        ctx.fillStyle = char.colors?.outfit || '#888888';\n   464\u2192        ctx.fillRect(cx - 3, py + 6, 6, 8);\n   465\u2192\n   466\u2192        // Head\n   467\u2192        ctx.fillStyle = char.colors?.body || '#ddccbb';\n   468\u2192        ctx.beginPath();\n   469\u2192        ctx.arc(cx, py + 4, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n   470\u2192        ctx.fill();\n   471\u2192\n   472\u2192        // Hair\n   473\u2192        ctx.fillStyle = char.colors?.hair || '#443322';\n   474\u2192        ctx.beginPath();\n   475\u2192        ctx.arc(cx, py + 3, 3, Math.PI, Math.PI * 2);\n   476\u2192        ctx.fill();\n   477\u2192      }\n   478\u2192\n   479\u2192      // Object-specific interaction particles\n   480\u2192      if (char.action === 'interacting') {\n   481\u2192        const particleType = getInteractParticleType(char);\n   482\u2192        this._maybeSpawnParticles(particleType, px + TILE_SIZE / 2, py + TILE_SIZE / 2);\n   483\u2192      }\n   484\u2192    }\n   485\u2192  }\n   486\u2192\n   487\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Character labels on text overlay (mood emoji + names) \u2500\u2500\n   488\u2192  renderCharacterLabels(characters, debug = false) {\n   489\u2192    if (!characters || characters.length === 0) return;\n   490\u2192    const ctx = this.textCtx;\n   491\u2192    const s = this.textScale;\n   492\u2192\n   493\u2192    for (const char of characters) {\n   494\u2192      const px = char.px * s;\n   495\u2192      const py = char.py * s;\n   496\u2192      const tileS = TILE_SIZE * s;\n   497\u2192\n   498\u2192      // Mood emoji above character\n   499\u2192      if (char.moodEmoji) {\n   500\u2192        ctx.font = `${Math.round(8 * s)}px serif`;\n   501\u2192        ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n   502\u2192        ctx.fillText(char.moodEmoji, px + tileS / 2, py - 1 * s);\n   503\u2192      }\n   504\u2192\n   505\u2192      // Name label below sprite\n   506\u2192      const fontSize = Math.round(5 * s);\n   507\u2192      ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;\n   508\u2192      ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n   509\u2192      const nameX = px + tileS / 2;\n   510\u2192      const nameY = py + tileS + 6 * s;\n   511\u2192\n   512\u2192      const label = debug ? `${char.name} [${char.action}]` : char.name;\n   513\u2192      const metrics = ctx.measureText(label);\n   514\u2192      const labelW = metrics.width + 3 * s;\n   515\u2192\n   516\u2192      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.6)';\n   517\u2192      ctx.fillRect(nameX - labelW / 2, nameY - 5 * s, labelW, 7 * s);\n   518\u2192\n   519\u2192      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n   520\u2192      ctx.fillText(label, nameX, nameY);\n   521\u2192    }\n   522\u2192  }\n   523\u2192\n   524\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Object labels (debug overlay) \u2500\u2500\n   525\u2192  renderObjectLabels(objects) {\n   526\u2192    const ctx = this.textCtx;\n   527\u2192    const s = this.textScale;\n   528\u2192    const fontSize = Math.round(5 * s);\n   529\u2192    ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;\n   530\u2192    ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n   531\u2192\n   532\u2192    for (const obj of objects) {\n   533\u2192      const tx = obj.position.tx;\n   534\u2192      const ty = obj.position.ty;\n   535\u2192      const pxX = (tx * TILE_SIZE + ((obj.position.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE) / 2) * s;\n   536\u2192      const pxY = (ty * TILE_SIZE - 2) * s;\n   537\u2192\n   538\u2192      const text = `${obj.name} [${obj.state}]`;\n   539\u2192      const metrics = ctx.measureText(text);\n   540\u2192      const textW = metrics.width + 4 * s;\n   541\u2192\n   542\u2192      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)';\n   543\u2192      ctx.fillRect(pxX - textW / 2, pxY - 5 * s, textW, 7 * s);\n   544\u2192\n   545\u2192      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n   546\u2192      ctx.fillText(text, pxX, pxY);\n   547\u2192\n   548\u2192      // Timer bar under object\n   549\u2192      if (obj.autoNextDuration !== null) {\n   550\u2192        const remaining = obj.timeRemainingMs;\n   551\u2192        const total = obj.autoNextDuration;\n   552\u2192        const pct = (total - remaining) / total;\n   553\u2192        const barW = ((obj.position.tw || 1) * TILE_SIZE - 4) * s;\n   554\u2192        const barY = ((ty + (obj.position.th || 1)) * TILE_SIZE + 1) * s;\n   555\u2192        const barX = (tx * TILE_SIZE + 2) * s;\n   556\u2192\n   557\u2192        ctx.fillStyle = '#333333';\n   558\u2192        ctx.fillRect(barX, barY, barW, 2 * s);\n   559\u2192        ctx.fillStyle = pct > 0.85 ? '#d04020' : pct > 0.66 ? '#d0a020' : '#40a040';\n   560\u2192        ctx.fillRect(barX, barY, barW * pct, 2 * s);\n   561\u2192      }\n   562\u2192    }\n   563\u2192  }\n   564\u2192\n   565\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Particles \u2500\u2500\n   566\u2192  _maybeSpawnParticles(type, x, y) {\n   567\u2192    const def = PARTICLE_DEFS[type];\n   568\u2192    if (!def) return;\n   569\u2192    const active = this.particles.filter(p => p.type === type).length;\n   570\u2192    if (active >= def.count * 2) return;\n   571\u2192\n   572\u2192    for (let i = 0; i < def.count; i++) {\n   573\u2192      const color = def.colors\n   574\u2192        ? def.colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * def.colors.length)]\n   575\u2192        : def.color;\n   576\u2192\n   577\u2192      let vx, vy;\n   578\u2192      if (def.dir === 'down') {\n   579\u2192        vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;\n   580\u2192        vy = def.speed + Math.random() * 0.2;\n   581\u2192      } else if (def.dir === 'radial') {\n   582\u2192        const angle = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;\n   583\u2192        vx = Math.cos(angle) * def.speed;\n   584\u2192        vy = Math.sin(angle) * def.speed;\n   585\u2192      } else {\n   586\u2192        vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;\n   587\u2192        vy = -def.speed - Math.random() * 0.2;\n   588\u2192      }\n   589\u2192\n   590\u2192      this.particles.push({\n   591\u2192        type,\n   592\u2192        x: x + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 8,\n   593\u2192        y: y,\n   594\u2192        vx,\n   595\u2192        vy,\n   596\u2192        life: def.life * (0.7 + Math.random() * 0.6),\n   597\u2192        maxLife: def.life,\n   598\u2192        color,\n   599\u2192        size: def.size,\n   600\u2192        shape: def.shape || 'circle',\n   601\u2192        wobble: def.wobble || false,\n   602\u2192        phase: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,\n   603\u2192        age: 0,\n   604\u2192      });\n   605\u2192    }\n   606\u2192  }\n   607\u2192\n   608\u2192  renderParticles(dt) {\n   609\u2192    const ctx = this.ctx;\n   610\u2192\n   611\u2192    for (let i = this.particles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n   612\u2192      const p = this.particles[i];\n   613\u2192      p.life -= dt;\n   614\u2192      if (p.life <= 0) {\n   615\u2192        this.particles.splice(i, 1);\n   616\u2192        continue;\n   617\u2192      }\n   618\u2192\n   619\u2192      p.x += p.vx;\n   620\u2192      p.y += p.vy;\n   621\u2192      p.age = (p.age || 0) + dt;\n   622\u2192\n   623\u2192      const alpha = Math.max(0, p.life / p.maxLife);\n   624\u2192      ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;\n   625\u2192      ctx.fillStyle = p.color;\n   626\u2192\n   627\u2192      // Sine wave wobble for steam/smoke\n   628\u2192      const drawX = p.wobble\n   629\u2192        ? p.x + Math.sin(p.age * 0.006 + (p.phase || 0)) * 1.5\n   630\u2192        : p.x;\n   631\u2192\n   632\u2192      if (p.shape === 'square') {\n   633\u2192        ctx.fillRect(drawX - p.size / 2, p.y - p.size / 2, p.size, p.size);\n   634\u2192      } else {\n   635\u2192        ctx.beginPath();\n   636\u2192        ctx.arc(drawX, p.y, p.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n   637\u2192        ctx.fill();\n   638\u2192      }\n   639\u2192    }\n   640\u2192\n   641\u2192    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;\n   642\u2192  }\n   643\u2192\n   644\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Speech Bubble \u2500\u2500\n   645\u2192  addSpeechBubble(tx, ty, text, durationMs = 3000) {\n   646\u2192    this.speechBubbles.push({\n   647\u2192      x: tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2,\n   648\u2192 Add a speech bubble attached to a character (follows their position). */\n   656\u2192  addCharacterSpeech(character, text, durationMs = 5000) {\n   657\u2192    // Remove any existing bubble for this character\n   658\u2192    this.speechBubbles = this.speechBubbles.filter(b => b.character !== character);\n   659\u2192\n   660\u2192    // Truncate long text for the tiny canvas\n   661\u2192    const maxLen = 60;\n   662\u2192    const truncated = text.length > maxLen ? text.substring(0, maxLen - 1) + '\\u2026' : text;\n   663\u2192\n   664\u2192    this.speechBubbles.push({\n   665\u2192      character,\n   666\u2192      text: truncated,\n   667\u2192      life: durationMs,\n   668\u2192      maxLife: durationMs,\n   669\u2192    });\n   670\u2192  }\n   671\u2192\n   672\u2192  setStatus(text) {\n   673\u2192    this.statusText = text;\n   674\u2192  }\n   675\u2192\n   676\u2192  _wrapText(ctx, text, maxWidth) {\n   677\u2192    const words = text.split(' ');\n   678\u2192    const lines = [];\n   679\u2192    let current = '';\n   680\u2192\n   681\u2192    for (const word of words) {\n   682\u2192      const test = current ? current + ' ' + word : word;\n   683\u2192      if (ctx.measureText(test).width > maxWidth && current) {\n   684\u2192        lines.push(current);\n   685\u2192        current = word;\n   686\u2192      } else {\n   687\u2192        current = test;\n   688\u2192      }\n   689\u2192    }\n   690\u2192    if (current) lines.push(current);\n   691\u2192    return lines.length > 0 ? lines : [text];\n   692\u2192  }\n   693\u2192\n   694\u2192  renderSpeechBubbles(dt) {\n   695\u2192    const ctx = this.textCtx;\n   696\u2192    const s = this.textScale;\n   697\u2192    const fontSize = Math.round(5 * s);\n   698\u2192    ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;\n   699\u2192    ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n   700\u2192\n   701\u2192    for (let i = this.speechBubbles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n   702\u2192      const b = this.speechBubbles[i];\n   703\u2192      b.life -= dt;\n   704\u2192      if (b.life <= 0) {\n   705\u2192        this.speechBubbles.splice(i, 1);\n   706\u2192        continue;\n   707\u2192      }\n   708\u2192\n   709\u2192      // Calculate anchor position (native coords scaled to text canvas)\n   710\u2192      let anchorX, anchorY;\n   711\u2192      if (b.character) {\n   712\u2192        anchorX = (b.character.px + TILE_SIZE / 2) * s;\n   713\u2192        anchorY = (b.character.py - 10) * s;\n   714\u2192      } else {\n   715\u2192        anchorX = b.x * s;\n   716\u2192        anchorY = b.y * s;\n   717\u2192      }\n   718\u2192\n   719\u2192      const alpha = Math.min(1, b.life / 500);\n   720\u2192      ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;\n   721\u2192\n   722\u2192      // Word wrap\n   723\u2192      const maxBubbleW = 100 * s;\n   724\u2192      const lines = this._wrapText(ctx, b.text, maxBubbleW - 8 * s);\n   725\u2192      const lineH = 7 * s;\n   726\u2192      const ctx.measureText(line).width;\n   732\u2192        if (w > maxLineW) maxLineW = w;\n   733\u2192      }\n   734\u2192\n   735\u2192      const bw = maxLineW + padX * 2;\n   736\u2192      const bh = bx = Math.max(s, Math.min(bx, this.textCanvas.width - bw - s));\n   742\u2192\n   743\u2192      // Background\n   744\u2192      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';\n   745\u2192      ctx.beginPath();\n   746\u2192      ctx.roundRect(bx, by, bw, bh, 3 * s);\n   747\u2192      ctx.fill();\n   748\u2192\n   749\u2192      // Tail\n   750\u2192      const tailX = Math.max(bx + 4 * s, Math.min(anchorX, bx + bw - 4 * s));\n   751\u2192      ctx.beginPath();\n   752\u2192      ctx.moveTo(tailX - 3 * s, by + bh);\n   753\u2192      ctx.lineTo(tailX, by + bh + 4 * s);\n   754\u2192      ctx.lineTo(tailX + 3 * s, by + bh);\n   755\u2192      ctx.fill();\n   756\u2192\n   757\u2192      // Text lines\n   758\u2192      ctx.fillStyle = '#222222';\n   759\u2192      for (let l = 0; l < lines.length; l++) }\n   766\u2192\n   767\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Status Bar \u2500\u2500\n   768\u2192  renderStatusBar() {\n   769\u2192    if (!this.statusText) return;\n   770\u2192\n   771\u2192    const ctx = this.textCtx;\n   772\u2192    const s = this.textScale;\n   773\u2192    const tw = this.textCanvas.width;\n   774\u2192    const th = this.textCanvas.height;\n   775\u2192    const barH = 12 * s;\n Truncate if too wide\n   787\u2192    let text = this.statusText;\n   788\u2192    while (ctx.measureText(text).width > tw - 8 * s && text.length > 10) {\n   789\u2192      text = text.substring(0, \u2500\u2500\n   796\u2192  addEmojiFloat(tx, ty, emoji) {\n   797\u2192    this.emojiFloats.push({\n   798\u2192      x: tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2,\n   799\u2192      y: ty * TILE_SIZE,\n   800\u2192      emoji,\n   801\u2192      life: 1500,\n   802\u2192      maxLife: 1500,\n   803\u2192    });\n   804\u2192  }\n   805\u2192\n   806\u2192  renderEmojiFloats(dt) {\n   807\u2192    const this.emojiFloats.splice(i, 1);\n   817\u2192        continue;\n   818\u2192      }\n   819\u2192\n   820\u2192      const progress = 1 - e.life / e.maxLife;\n   821\u2192      const alpha = 1 -  }\n   827\u2192\n   828\u2192    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;\n   829\u2192  }\n   830\u2192\n   831\u2192  // \u2500\u2500 Highlight a tile (for hover/click feedback) \u2500\u2500\n   832\u2192 ASSISTANTMESSAGE #17
Now I need to understand the issue more clearly. The issue says: 1. Objects stay as their default sprite even when state changes (stove stays as stove_off.png, books stay closed, easel stays blank) 2. What needs to happen: - Define a sprite map per object: { stateName: spriteKey } - On each state transition (in objectEngine), emit the new sprite key - Scene.js swaps the sprite texture on the Phaser game object - Map: stove cooking/done->stove_on, idle->stove_off; bookshelf reading->book_open, idle->book_closed; easel painting->easel_painting, done->easel_finished, idle->easel_blank; tea_set brewing/ready->cup_full, idle->cup_empty Actually, looking at the code more carefully, this is canvas-based, not Phaser. The `ObjectInstance` class already has a `visual` getter that returns the current state definition's visual property or falls back to the state name, and the renderer uses this to look up the sprite from the sprite map. So the infrastructure for sprite swapping is already there—I just need to make sure the visual property is being set correctly when state changes.

The `ObjectInstance` class already has a `visual` getter that returns the current state definition's visual property or falls back to the state name, and the renderer uses this to look up the sprite from the sprite map. So the infrastructure for sprite swapping is already there\u2014I just need to make sure the visual property is being set correctly when state changes.",
