     1→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     2→// Main Simulation Engine
     3→// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     4→//
     5→// Manages the game clock and drives the object engine + characters.
     6→// Ticks at configurable intervals (~5 seconds default).
     7→// Provides start/stop/pause controls and an event bus.
     8→
     9→import { ObjectEngine } from './objects.js';
    10→import { OBJECT_DEFS, SECTORS, WORLD_TREE } from './world.js';
    11→import { Character, CHARACTER_DEFS, findInteractTile } from './characters.js';
    12→
    13→export class SimulationEngine {
    14→  constructor(options = {}) {
    15→    this.tickIntervalMs = options.tickIntervalMs ?? 5000; // ~5 seconds
    16→    this.timeScale = options.timeScale ?? 1;              // speed multiplier
    17→
    18→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    19→    this.running = false;
    20→    this.paused = false;
    21→    this.elapsedMs = 0;         // total simulation time
    22→    this.tickCount = 0;
    23→    this.listeners = new Map();  // event type → Set<callback>
    24→
    25→    this._rafId = null;
    26→    this._lastTimestamp = null;
    27→    this._accumulator = 0;       // accumulated time toward next tick
    28→
    29→    // Load world
    30→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    31→    this.sectors = SECTORS;
    32→    this.worldTree = WORLD_TREE;
    33→
    34→    // Load characters
    35→    this.characters = CHARACTER_DEFS.map(def => new Character(def));
    36→
    37→    // AI integration
    38→    this.aiEngine = options.aiEngine || null;
    39→    this.aiMode = false;
    40→
    41→    // Simulated clock — starts at 8:00 AM on Day 1
    42→    // Each tick advances 5 sim-minutes → 1 sim-day per ~24 real minutes at 1x
    43→    this.simClock = {
    44→      day: 1,
    45→      minuteOfDay: 480,
    46→      simMinutesPerTick: 5,
    47→      get hour() { return Math.floor(this.minuteOfDay / 60); },
    48→      get minute() { return Math.floor(this.minuteOfDay % 60); },
    49→      get timeString() {
    50→        const h = this.hour;
    51→        const m = this.minute;
    52→        const period = h >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
    53→        const h12 = h % 12 || 12;
    54→        return `${h12}:${String(m).padStart(2, '0')} ${period}`;
    55→      },
    56→      get dayTimeString() {
    57→        return `Day ${this.day} \u2014 ${this.timeString}`;
    58→      },
    59→      advance() {
    60→        this.minuteOfDay += this.simMinutesPerTick;
    61→        while (this.minuteOfDay >= 1440) {
    62→          this.minuteOfDay -= 1440;
    63→          this.day++;
    64→        }
    65→      },
    66→    };
    67→
    68→    // Last notable event for the status bar
    69→    this.lastStatusText = '';
    70→
    71→    // Forward object events to our bus
    72→    this.objectEngine.onTransition((event) => {
    73→      this._emit('object:transition', event);
    74→      this._reactToObjectEvent(event);
    75→    });
    76→
    77→    // Attach AI engine
    78→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    79→      this.aiEngine.attach(this);
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  start() {
    84→    if (this.running) return;
    85→    this.running = true;
    86→    this.paused = false;
    87→    this._lastTimestamp = performance.now();
    88→    this._accumulator = 0;
    89→    this._emit('engine:start', { elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs });
    90→    this._loop();
    91→  }
    92→
    93→  stop() {
    94→    this.running = false;
    95→    this.paused = false;
    96→    if (this._rafId) {
    97→      cancelAnimationFrame(this._rafId);
    98→      this._rafId = null;
    99→    }
   100→    this._emit('engine:stop', { elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs, tickCount: this.tickCount });
   101→  }
   102→
   103→  pause() {
   104→    if (!this.running) return;
   105→    this.paused = true;
   106→    this._emit('engine:pause', { elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs });
   107→  }
   108→
   109→  resume() {
   110→    if (!this.running || !this.paused) return;
   111→    this.paused = false;
   112→    this._lastTimestamp = performance.now();
   113→    this._emit('engine:resume', { elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs });
   114→  }
   115→
   116→  // Manually advance by a number of ticks (useful for testing)
   117→  manualTick(count = 1) {
   118→    const events = [];
   119→    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   120→      const tickEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(this.tickIntervalMs);
   121→      this.tickCount++;
   122→      this.elapsedMs += this.tickIntervalMs;
   123→      this._wanderTick();
   124→      this._updateCharacters(this.tickIntervalMs);
   125→      events.push(...tickEvents);
   126→    }
   127→    this._emit('engine:tick', {
   128→      tickCount: this.tickCount,
   129→      elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs,
   130→      events,
   131→    });
   132→    return events;
   133→  }
   134→
   135→  // Interact with an object (character-triggered)
   136→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   137→    return this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   138→  }
   139→
   140→  // Get object by id
   141→  getObject(objectId) {
   142→    return this.objectEngine.get(objectId);
   143→  }
   144→
   145→  // Get all objects
   146→  getAllObjects() {
   147→    return this.objectEngine.getAll();
   148→  }
   149→
   150→  // Get objects in a sector
   151→  getObjectsInSector(sector) {
   152→    return this.objectEngine.getBySector(sector);
   153→  }
   154→
   155→  // Get all characters
   156→  getCharacters() {
   157→    return this.characters;
   158→  }
   159→
   160→  // Full state snapshot
   161→  snapshot() {
   162→    return {
   163→      running: this.running,
   164→      paused: this.paused,
   165→      elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs,
   166→      tickCount: this.tickCount,
   167→      tickIntervalMs: this.tickIntervalMs,
   168→      timeScale: this.timeScale,
   169→      aiMode: this.aiMode,
   170→      simClock: { day: this.simClock.day, time: this.simClock.timeString },
   171→      objects: this.objectEngine.snapshot(),
   172→      characters: this.characters.map(c => ({
   173→        id: c.id, name: c.name, tx: c.tx, ty: c.ty,
   174→        action: c.action, facing: c.facing, mood: c.mood,
   175→        targetObjectId: c.targetObjectId,
   176→      })),
   177→    };
   178→  }
   179→
   180→  // ── Event bus ──
   181→
   182→  on(eventType, callback) {
   183→    if (!this.listeners.has(eventType)) {
   184→      this.listeners.set(eventType, new Set());
   185→    }
   186→    this.listeners.get(eventType).add(callback);
   187→    return () => this.off(eventType, callback);
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  off(eventType, callback) {
   191→    this.listeners.get(eventType)?.delete(callback);
   192→  }
   193→
   194→  _emit(eventType, data) {
   195→    const callbacks = this.listeners.get(eventType);
   196→    if (callbacks) {
   197→      for (const cb of callbacks) {
   198→        cb(data);
   199→      }
   200→    }
   201→    // Also emit wildcard
   202→    const wildcards = this.listeners.get('*');
   203→    if (wildcards) {
   204→      for (const cb of wildcards) {
   205→        cb({ type: eventType, ...data });
   206→      }
   207→    }
   208→  }
   209→
   210→  // ── Character AI / Wander behavior ──
   211→
   212→  _wanderTick() {
   213→    // Advance simulated clock each tick
   214→    this.simClock.advance();
   215→
   216→    for (const char of this.characters) {
   217→      if (char.action !== 'idle') continue;
   218→
   219→      // AI mode: delegate to AI decision engine
   220→      if (this.aiMode && this.aiEngine) {
   221→        if (!this.aiEngine.isPending(char.id)) {
   222→          this.aiEngine.tick(char, this.tickIntervalMs);
   223→        }
   224→        continue;
   225→      }
   226→
   227→      // Random wander with cooldown
   228→      char.wanderCooldown -= this.tickIntervalMs;
   229→      if (char.wanderCooldown > 0) continue;
   230→
   231→      // Priority actions first (reactive behavior), then random wander
   232→      const priority = this._getPriorityTarget(char);
   233→      const target = priority ? priority.obj : this._pickWanderTarget(char);
   234→      const action = priority ? priority.action : 'use';
   235→
   236→      if (!target) {
   237→        char.wanderCooldown = 5000;
   238→        continue;
   239→      }
   240→
   241→      const tile = findInteractTile(target.position);
   242→      if (!tile) {
   243→        char.wanderCooldown = 5000;
   244→        continue;
   245→      }
   246→
   247→      // Already adjacent — interact directly
   248→      const atTarget = tile.tx === Math.round(char.tx) && tile.ty === Math.round(char.ty);
   249→      if (atTarget) {
   250→        this._doInteraction(char, target, action);
   251→        char.wanderCooldown = 30000 + Math.random() * 30000;
   252→      } else if (char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   253→        char.targetObjectId = target.id;
   254→        char.pendingAction = action;
   255→        char.wanderCooldown = 30000 + Math.random() * 30000;
   256→      } else {
   257→        char.wanderCooldown = 5000;
   258→      }
   259→    }
   260→  }
   261→
   262→  /** Immediate random wander (no cooldown) — used as AI fallback. */
   263→  _randomWander(char) {
   264→    const priority = this._getPriorityTarget(char);
   265→    const target = priority ? priority.obj : this._pickWanderTarget(char);
   266→    const action = priority ? priority.action : 'use';
   267→
   268→    if (!target) return;
   269→
   270→    const tile = findInteractTile(target.position);
   271→    if (!tile) return;
   272→
   273→    const atTarget = tile.tx === Math.round(char.tx) && tile.ty === Math.round(char.ty);
   274→    if (atTarget) {
   275→      this._doInteraction(char, target, action);
   276→    } else if (char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   277→      char.targetObjectId = target.id;
   278→      char.pendingAction = action;
   279→    }
   280→  }
   281→
   282→  _updateCharacters(deltaMs) {
   283→    for (const char of this.characters) {
   284→      const wasWalking = char.action === 'walking';
   285→      char.update(deltaMs);
   286→
   287→      // Character just arrived at destination
   288→      if (wasWalking && char.action === 'idle') {
   289→        if (char.targetObjectId) {
   290→          const obj = this.objectEngine.get(char.targetObjectId);
   291→          if (obj) {
   292→            this._doInteraction(char, obj, char.pendingAction || 'use');
   293→          } else {
   294→            char.targetObjectId = null;
   295→          }
   296→          char.pendingAction = 'use';
   297→        } else if (char.targetCharId) {
   298→          // Character arrived near another character for conversation — face each other
   299→          const target = this.characters.find(c => c.id === char.targetCharId);
   300→          if (target) {
   301→            char._updateFacing(target.tx - char.tx, target.ty - char.ty);
   302→            target._updateFacing(char.tx - target.tx, char.ty - target.ty);
   303→          }
   304→          char.targetCharId = null;
   305→        }
   306→      }
   307→    }
   308→  }
   309→
   310→  // ── Object → interaction animation mapping ──
   311→  // Maps object ID substrings to the animation played during interaction.
   312→  static _getInteractAnim(objectId) {
   313→    if (!objectId) return null;
   314→    if (objectId.includes('book') || objectId.includes('desk') || objectId.includes('bookshelf')) {
   315→      return 'reading';
   316→    }
   317→    if (objectId.includes('bed') || objectId.includes('kotatsu') || objectId.includes('sofa') || objectId.includes('tv')) {
   318→      return 'sit';
   319→    }
   320→    // phone / general interaction fallback for everything else
   321→    return 'phone';
   322→  }
   323→
   324→  _doInteraction(char, obj, action = 'use') {
   325→    // Face toward the object
   326→    const objCx = obj.position.tx + (obj.position.tw || 1) / 2;
   327→    const objCy = obj.position.ty + (obj.position.th || 1) / 2;
   328→    const dx = objCx - char.tx;
   329→    const dy = objCy - char.ty;
   330→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   331→      char._updateFacing(dx, 0);
   332→    } else {
   333→      char._updateFacing(0, dy);
   334→    }
   335→
   336→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(obj.id, action);
   337→    if (event) {
   338→      const anim = SimulationEngine._getInteractAnim(obj.id);
   339→      char.startInteraction(obj.id, anim);
   340→
   341→      // Successful interaction → happy (unless already upset)
   342→      if (char.mood !== 'upset') {
   343→        char.setMood('happy', 5000);
   344→      }
   345→
   346→      this._emit('character:interact', {
   347→        characterId: char.id, characterName: char.name,
   348→        objectId: obj.id, objectName: event.objectName,
   349→        from: event.from, to: event.to,
   350→        produces: event.produces || null,
   351→        emoji: event.emoji || null,
   352→      });
   353→    } else {
   354→      char.targetObjectId = null;
   355→    }
   356→  }
   357→
   358→  _getPriorityTarget(char) {
   359→    // Sol: pick up book if closed and nearby
   360→    if (char.id === 'sol') {
   361→      const book = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_book');
   362→      if (book && book.state === 'closed') {
   363→        const dist = Math.abs(book.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(book.position.ty - char.ty);
   364→        if (dist <= 6) {
   365→          return { obj: book, action: 'use' };
   366→        }
   367→      }
   368→    }
   369→
   370→    // Non-Maple near stocked display → take pastry
   371→    if (char.id !== 'maple') {
   372→      const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   373→      if (display && display.state === 'stocked') {
   374→        const dist = Math.abs(display.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(display.position.ty - char.ty);
   375→        if (dist <= 8) {
   376→          return { obj: display, action: 'use' };
   377→        }
   378→      }
   379→    }
   380→
   381→    // Maple: restock empty display case
   382→    if (char.id === 'maple') {
   383→      const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   384→      if (display && display.state === 'empty') {
   385→        return { obj: display, action: 'use' };
   386→      }
   387→    }
   388→
   389→    return null;
   390→  }
   391→
   392→  _pickWanderTarget(char) {
   393→    const allObjects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   394→
   395→    // 60% home sector, 40% any sector
   396→    let candidates;
   397→    if (Math.random() < 0.6) {
   398→      candidates = allObjects.filter(o => o.sector === char.homeSector);
   399→      if (candidates.length === 0) candidates = allObjects;
   400→    } else {
   401→      candidates = allObjects;
   402→    }
   403→
   404→    // Avoid repeating last interaction
   405→    if (char.lastObjectId && candidates.length > 1) {
   406→      candidates = candidates.filter(o => o.id !== char.lastObjectId);
   407→    }
   408→
   409→    if (candidates.length === 0) return null;
   410→    return candidates[Math.floor(Math.random() * candidates.length)];
   411→  }
   412→
   413→  _reactToObjectEvent(event) {
   414→    // Espresso done → Maple happy
   415→    if (event.objectId === 'cafe_espresso' && event.to === 'done') {
   416→      const maple = this.characters.find(c => c.id === 'maple');
   417→      if (maple) maple.setMood('happy', 10000);
   418→    }
   419→
   420→    // Easel finished → Nyx happy
   421→    if (event.objectId === 'apt_easel' && event.to === 'finished') {
   422→      const nyx = this.characters.find(c => c.id === 'nyx');
   423→      if (nyx) nyx.setMood('happy', 20000);
   424→    }
   425→
   426→    // Display restocked → nearby characters happy
   427→    if (event.objectId === 'cafe_display' && event.to === 'stocked') {
   428→      for (const char of this.characters) {
   429→        const display = this.objectEngine.get('cafe_display');
   430→        if (display) {
   431→          const dist = Math.abs(display.position.tx - char.tx) + Math.abs(display.position.ty - char.ty);
   432→          if (dist <= 6) char.setMood('happy', 10000);
   433→        }
   434→      }
   435→    }
   436→  }
   437→
   438→  // ── Internal loop ──
   439→
   440→  _loop() {
   441→    if (!this.running) return;
   442→
   443→    this._rafId = requestAnimationFrame((timestamp) => {
   444→      if (!this.running) return;
   445→
   446→      if (!this.paused) {
   447→        const rawDelta = timestamp - this._lastTimestamp;
   448→        const delta = Math.min(rawDelta, 500) * this.timeScale; // cap delta, apply scale
   449→
   450→        this._accumulator += delta;
   451→
   452→        // Process full ticks
   453→        while (this._accumulator >= this.tickIntervalMs) {
   454→          this._accumulator -= this.tickIntervalMs;
   455→          const tickEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(this.tickIntervalMs);
   456→          this.tickCount++;
   457→          this.elapsedMs += this.tickIntervalMs;
   458→
   459→          this._wanderTick();
   460→
   461→          this._emit('engine:tick', {
   462→            tickCount: this.tickCount,
   463→            elapsedMs: this.elapsedMs,
   464→            events: tickEvents,
   465→          });
   466→        }
   467→
   468→        // Smooth character movement each frame
   469→        this._updateCharacters(delta);
   470→      }
   471→
   472→      this._lastTimestamp = timestamp;
   473→      this._loop();
   474→    });
   475→  }
   476→}

   258→import { Renderer, preloadSprites } from './src/renderer.js';
   259→import { TILE_SIZE } from './src/tilemap.js';
   260→import { WORLD_TREE } from './src/world.js';
   261→import { AIDecisionEngine } from './src/ai.js';
   262→import { AudioEngine } from './src/audio.js';
   263→
   264→// ── AI setup ──
   265→const aiEngine = new AIDecisionEngine();
   266→
   267→// ── Audio setup ──
   268→const audio = new AudioEngine();
   269→// Restore mute preference
   270→const savedMute = localStorage.getItem('ai-aquarium-muted');
   271→if (savedMute === 'true') {
   272→  audio.muted = true;
   273→}
   274→
   275→// ── State ──
   276→let engine = new SimulationEngine({ aiEngine });
   277→let debugVisible = false;
   278→const eventLog = [];
   279→const MAX_LOG = 30;
   280→
   281→// ── Renderer setup ──
   282→const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
   283→const renderer = new Renderer(container);
   284→
   285→// ── DOM refs ──
   286→const $ = (id) => document.getElementById(id);
   287→const debugOverlay = $('debug-overlay');
   288→const tooltip = $('click-tooltip');
   289→
   290→// ── Debug toggle ──
   291→document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
   292→  if (e.key === 'd' || e.key === 'D') {
   293→    debugVisible = !debugVisible;
   294→    debugOverlay.classList.toggle('visible', debugVisible);
   295→  }
   296→});
   297→
   298→// ── Engine event listeners ──
   299→function attachEngineListeners() {
   300→  engine.on('object:transition', (event) => {
   301→    eventLog.unshift(event);
   302→    if (eventLog.length > MAX_LOG) eventLog.pop();
   303→    renderDebugLog();
   304→
   305→    // Trigger emoji float on the renderer
   306→    if (event.emoji) {
   307→      const obj = engine.getObject(event.objectId);
   308→      if (obj) {
   309→        renderer.addEmojiFloat(obj.position.tx, obj.position.ty, event.emoji);
   310→      }
   311→    }
   312→  });
   313→
   314→  engine.on('character:interact', (event) => {
   315→    eventLog.unshift({
   316→      objectName: event.objectName,
   317→      from: event.from,
   318→      to: event.to,
   319→      trigger: event.characterName,
   320→      emoji: event.emoji || null,
   321→    });
   322→    if (eventLog.length > MAX_LOG) eventLog.pop();
   323→    renderDebugLog();
   324→
   325→    // Emoji float on character for production events
   326→    if (event.produces) {
   327→      const char = engine.getCharacters().find(c => c.id === event.characterId);
   328→      if (char) {
   329→        const emoji = event.produces === 'bread' ? '🍞' :
   330→                      event.produces === 'burnt_bread' ? '💨' : '✨';
   331→        renderer.addEmojiFloat(Math.round(char.tx), Math.round(char.ty), emoji);
   332→      }
   333→    }
   334→  });
   335→
   336→  engine.on('engine:tick', () => {
   337→    // Update status bar with sim clock + last event
   338→    const clock = engine.simClock;
   339→    const status = engine.lastStatusText || '';
   340→    const line = status
   341→      ? `${clock.dayTimeString} \u2014 ${status}`
   342→      : clock.dayTimeString;
   343→    renderer.setStatus(line);
   344→
   345→    // Sync audio ambient layers with time of day
   346→    audio.setTimeOfDay(clock.minuteOfDay);
   347→
   348→    renderDebugStatus();
   349→  });
   350→
   351→  engine.on('ai:speech', (event) => {
   352→    const char = engine.getCharacters().find(c => c.id === event.characterId);
   353→    if (char) {
   354→      renderer.addCharacterSpeech(char, event.dialogue, 5000);
   355→    }
   356→  });
   357→
   358→  engine.on('ai:status', (event) => {
   359→    engine.lastStatusText = `${event.characterName} ${event.description}`;
   360→  });
   361→}
   362→attachEngineListeners();
   363→
   364→// ── Debug controls ──
   365→$('startBtn').onclick = () => { engine.start(); renderDebugStatus(); };
   366→$('pauseBtn').onclick = () => {
   367→  if (engine.paused) engine.resume(); else engine.pause();
   368→  renderDebugStatus();
   369→};
   370→$('stopBtn').onclick = () => { engine.stop(); renderDebugStatus(); };
   371→$('tickBtn').onclick = () => { engine.manualTick(1); renderDebugStatus(); };
   372→$('tick10Btn').onclick = () => { engine.manualTick(10); renderDebugStatus(); };
   373→
   374→function setSpeed(scale) {
   375→  engine.timeScale = scale;
   376→  $('speed1Btn').classList.toggle('active', scale === 1);
   377→  $('speed5Btn').classList.toggle('active', scale === 5);
   378→  $('speed20Btn').classList.toggle('active', scale === 20);
   379→  renderDebugStatus();
   380→}
   381→$('speed1Btn').onclick = () => setSpeed(1);
   382→$('speed5Btn').onclick = () => setSpeed(5);
   383→$('speed20Btn').onclick = () => setSpeed(20);
   384→
   385→// ── AI controls ──
   386→const apiInput = $('apiEndpoint');
   387→const apiWarning = $('apiWarning');
   388→
   389→apiInput.addEventListener('change', () => {
   390→  const url = apiInput.value.trim();
   391→  aiEngine.setEndpoint(url);
   392→  apiWarning.style.display = url ? 'none' : 'inline';
   393→  if (engine.aiMode && !url) {
   394→    apiWarning.textContent = '\u26A0 AI on but no endpoint \u2014 will wander randomly';
   395→    apiWarning.style.display = 'inline';
   396→  }
   397→});
   398→
   399→$('aiToggleBtn').onclick = () => {
   400→  engine.aiMode = !engine.aiMode;
   401→  const btn = $('aiToggleBtn');
   402→  btn.textContent = `AI: ${engine.aiMode ? 'On' : 'Off'}`;
   403→  btn.classList.toggle('active', engine.aiMode);
   404→
   405→  const url = apiInput.value.trim();
   406→  if (engine.aiMode && !url) {
   407→    apiWarning.textContent = '\u26A0 AI on but no endpoint \u2014 will wander randomly';
   408→    apiWarning.style.display = 'inline';
   409→  } else if (url) {
   410→    apiWarning.style.display = 'none';
   411→  }
   412→  renderDebugStatus();
   413→};
   414→
   415→$('resetBtn').onclick = () => {
   416→  engine.stop();
   417→  engine = new SimulationEngine({ aiEngine });
   418→  // Preserve AI mode state across reset
   419→  const aiOn = $('aiToggleBtn').textContent.includes('On');
   420→  engine.aiMode = aiOn;
   421→  eventLog.length = 0;
   422→  attachEngineListeners();
   423→  renderDebugStatus();
   424→  renderDebugLog();
   425→  renderer.setStatus('');
   426→};
   427→
   428→// ── Debug status render ──
   429→function renderDebugStatus() {
   430→  const stateEl = $('engineState');
   431→  if (engine.running && !engine.paused) {
   432→    stateEl.textContent = 'running';
   433→    stateEl.className = 'running';
   434→  } else if (engine.paused) {
   435→    stateEl.textContent = 'paused';
   436→    stateEl.className = 'paused';
   437→  } else {
   438→    stateEl.textContent = 'stopped';
   439→    stateEl.className = 'stopped';
   440→  }
   441→  $('tickCount').textContent = engine.tickCount;
   442→  $('elapsedTime').textContent = formatMs(engine.elapsedMs);
   443→  $('timeScale').textContent = engine.timeScale + 'x';
   444→
   445→  $('simClockDisplay').textContent = engine.simClock.dayTimeString;
   446→  const aiDisplay = $('aiModeDisplay');
   447→  aiDisplay.textContent = engine.aiMode ? 'on' : 'off';
   448→  aiDisplay.style.color = engine.aiMode ? '#7c7' : '#c77';
   449→
   450→  renderCharStatus();
   451→}
   452→
   453→function renderDebugLog() {
   454→  const el = $('debugLog');
   455→  if (eventLog.length === 0) {
   456→    el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555">No events yet</div>';
   457→    return;
   458→  }
   459→  let html = '';
   460→  for (const e of eventLog) {
   461→    const emoji = e.emoji || '';
   462→    html += `<div class="entry">${emoji} <span class="obj-name">${e.objectName}</span>: <span class="from">${e.from}</span> → <span class="to">${e.to}</span> <span class="trigger">[${e.trigger}]</span></div>`;
   463→  }
   464→  el.innerHTML = html;
   465→}
   466→
   467→function renderCharStatus() {
   468→  const chars = engine.getCharacters();
   469→  let html = '<div style="color:#cc8; font-size:10px; margin-bottom:2px">Characters:</div>';
   470→  for (const c of chars) {
   471→    const target = c.targetObjectId ? ` <span class="char-target">→ ${c.targetObjectId}</span>` : '';
   472→    const moodIcon = c.moodEmoji || '';
   473→    const lastObj = c.lastObjectId ? ` <span style="color:#555">last:${c.lastObjectId}</span>` : '';
   474→    html += `<div style="padding:1px 0"><span class="char-label">${c.name}</span> ${moodIcon}: ` +
   475→      `<span class="char-action">${c.action}</span> ` +
   476→      `<span style="color:#686">[${c.mood}]</span> ` +
   477→      `(${Math.round(c.tx)},${Math.round(c.ty)})${target}${lastObj}</div>`;
   478→  }
   479→  $('charStatus').innerHTML = html;
   480→}
   481→
   482→// ── Canvas click → find object at tile → trigger interaction ──
   483→renderer.canvas.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   484→  const { tx, ty } = renderer.pageToTile(e.clientX, e.clientY);
   485→  const obj = findObjectAtTile(tx, ty);
   486→
   487→  if (obj) {
   488→    const stateDef = obj.currentStateDef;
   489→    if (stateDef?.transitions) {
   490→      // Pick first available action
   491→      const action = Object.keys(stateDef.transitions)[0];
   492→      if (action) {
   493→        engine.interact(obj.id, action);
   494→        renderDebugStatus();
   495→
   496→        // Show brief feedback
   497→        showTooltip(e.clientX, e.clientY, `${obj.name}: ${action}`);
   498→      }
   499→    } else {
   500→      showTooltip(e.clientX, e.clientY, `${obj.name} [${obj.state}] — no actions`);
   501→    }
   502→  }
   503→});
   504→
   505→// Right-click: show all available actions for multi-action objects
   506→renderer.canvas.addEventListener('contextmenu', (e) => {
   507→  e.preventDefault();
   508→  const { tx, ty } = renderer.pageToTile(e.clientX, e.clientY);
   509→  const obj = findObjectAtTile(tx, ty);
   510→
   511→  if (obj) {
   512→    const stateDef = obj.currentStateDef;
   513→    const actions = stateDef?.transitions ? Object.keys(stateDef.transitions) : [];
   514→    const timerInfo = obj.timeRemainingMs !== null
   515→      ? ` (${(obj.timeRemainingMs / 1000).toFixed(0)}s remaining)`
   516→      : '';
   517→    showTooltip(e.clientX, e.clientY,
   518→      `${obj.name} [${obj.state}]${timerInfo}
Actions: ${actions.length ? actions.join(', ') : 'none'}`,
   519→      2000
   520→    );
   521→  }
   522→});
   523→
   524→function findObjectAtTile(tx, ty) {
   525→  const objects = engine.getAllObjects();
   526→  for (const obj of objects) {
   527→    const otx = obj.position.tx;
   528→    const oty = obj.position.ty;
   529→    const otw = obj.position.tw || 1;
   530→    const oth = obj.position.th || 1;
   531→    if (tx >= otx && tx < otx + otw && ty >= oty && ty < oty + oth) {
   532→      return obj;
   533→    }
   534→  }
   535→  return null;
   536→}
   537→
   538→function showTooltip(x, y, text, duration = 1200) {
   539→  tooltip.style.left = (x + 12) + 'px';
   540→  tooltip.style.top = (y - 20) + 'px';
   541→  tooltip.textContent = text;
   542→  tooltip.style.display = 'block';
   543→  clearTimeout(tooltip._hideTimer);
   544→  tooltip._hideTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   545→    tooltip.style.display = 'none';
   546→  }, duration);
   547→}
   548→
   549→// ── Utilities ──
   550→function formatMs(ms) {
   551→  const totalSec = Math.floor(ms / 1000);
   552→  const min = Math.floor(totalSec / 60);
   553→  const sec = totalSec % 60;
   554→  return min > 0 ? `${min}m ${sec}s` : `${sec}s`;
   555→}
   556→
   557→// ── Preload sprites, then start render loop ──
   558→preloadSprites().then(sprites => {
   559→  renderer.setSprites(sprites);
   560→  console.log(`Sprites loaded: ${sprites.tiles.size} tiles, ${sprites.objects.size} objects, ${sprites.characters.size} characters`);
   561→}).catch(err => {
   562→  console.warn('Sprite preload failed, using color fallback:', err);
   563→}).finally(() => {
   564→  renderer.startLoop(
   565→    () => engine.getAllObjects(),
   566→    () => engine.getCharacters(),
   567→    { showDebug: () => debugVisible, getSimClock: () => engine.simClock }
   568→  );
   569→});
   570→
   571→// ── Click-to-start overlay ──
   572→const overlay = $('start-overlay');
   573→const muteBtn = $('mute-btn');
   574→
   575→overlay.addEventListener('click', () => {
   576→  overlay.classList.add('hidden');
   577→  muteBtn.textContent = audio.muted ? '🔇' : '🔊';
   578→  muteBtn.classList.add('visible');
   579→  engine.start();
   580→  audio.start();
   581→  renderDebugStatus();
   582→  console.log('AI Aquarium started');
   583→});
   584→
   585→// ── Mute toggle ──
   586→muteBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   587→  const muted = audio.toggleMute();
   588→  muteBtn.textContent = muted ? '🔇' : '🔊';
   589→  localStorage.setItem('ai-aquarium-muted', muted);
   590→});
   591→
   592→// ── Initial state ──
   593→renderDebugStatus();
   594→renderDebugLog();
   595→
   596→console.log('AI Aquarium — Click to start');
   597→console.log('Objects:', engine.getAllObjects().map(o => `${o.id} [${o.state}]`).join(', '));
   598→console.log('Characters:', engine.getCharacters().map(c => `${c.name} at (${c.tx},${c.ty})`).join(', '));
   599→</script>
   600→</body>
   601→</html>

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #31
Now I understand the full picture. The renderer calls `engine.getAllObjects()` each frame, which returns live `ObjectInstance` objects that have the `visual` getter. So the rendering chain should work correctly. Looking at the current state: 1. `apt_stove` has proper `visual` per state: `stove_off` (off) and `stove_on` (heating/cooking/done) 2. `cafe_book` has proper `visual` per state: `book_closed` (closed) and `book_open` (reading) 3. `apt_easel` has proper `visual` per state: `easel_blank`, `easel_painting`, `easel_finished` But wait, the issue says objects don't change sprite when state transitions, so something's not working as expected. Let me look more carefully at the world.js configuration to see what's actually defined for each state. Looking at the stove object, each state has a `visual` property that maps to the correct sprite name, and the `ObjectInstance` getter should return that visual. But I'm noticing the `tea_set` object is missing entirely from the world definition, which the issue mentions should be there. Also, there's a mismatch with the bookshelf - the sprite map references `cafe_book` but the visuals should map to `book_closed` and `book_open`. I think the real problem might not be in the state definitions themselves, but in how the renderer is actually looking up which sprite to display based on the current state. The stove stays as stove_off.png even when its state is cooking or done. Books stay closed. Easel stays blank. Object state machines work internally but have no visual feedback.

No changes were needed there. - **Tea set position `{ tx:13, ty:3 }`**: Placed on a kitchen dark-floor tile (row 3, col 13) one row below the stove/fridge row — avoids overlap with existing objects while staying in the kitchen zone. - **`ready` state auto-returns to `idle`**: Ensures sprites swap back to default (`cup_empty`) after 60s without manual interaction, satisfying the "sprites swap back to default" acceptance criterion. ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-246-object-sprite-state-transitions` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium/pull/6
